# PVP Token Finder - Features - Talk.Markets

[PVP Token Finder](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-token-finder/8152)

=================================================================

[Rick Bot](https://talk.markets/c/rick/61) [Features](https://talk.markets/c/rick/features/71)

[telegram](https://talk.markets/tag/telegram)
, [beta](https://talk.markets/tag/beta)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   3 January 2026 00:20 1

**PVP Finder** shows **$TICKER** matches that fit various criteria. The goal is to quickly see **relevant** tokens of interest. Only supported on ![:sol:](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/4/4871e9fc071dc845d033bcbc5807ddf0be63bbae.png?v=15 ":sol:") [Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)
.

> \[!tg\] If beta is enabled, PVP tokens will shown on tokens not older then 24h. **To opt into beta, use `/beta on`.**

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-token-finder/8152#p-21681-usage-1)
Usage
======================================================================

If your group enabled [beta](https://talk.markets/tag/beta)
, PVPs are **automatically** shown on tokens **younger than 24h**.

To see PVPs for **older** tokens, use `/pvp <symbol OR address>` or simply `/pvp` **in reply to** a token scan.

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-token-finder/8152#p-21681-line-definitions-2)
Line Definitions
============================================================================================

Results are sorted by **FDV**. Click **the age** for token info.

 **![:crossed_swords:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/crossed_swords.png?v=15 ":crossed_swords:") PVP matches**  
↳ `AGE` ⋅ `FDV` ⇨ `ATH` ⋅ 1H: `VOL`  
↳ **20m** ⋅ `25K` ⇨ `52K` ⋅ 1H: `192K`

> \[!info\] There may be more ticker matches, Rick only shows results that are **relevant enough** to display.

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-token-finder/8152#p-21681-feedback-3)
Feedback
============================================================================

Please use `/burpback <feedback>` in reply to a token scan to give feedback; like missing tokens, tokens that shouldn’t be there, or any other thoughts.

_After the beta, I will explore multi-chain PVP’s and allow deeplinking to this command._

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-token-finder/8152#p-21681-preview-4)
Preview
==========================================================================

[![Example PVP matches output](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/a/a268ba7222508996cbf82d1d5c9f80568e7330ac.jpeg)\
\
Example PVP matches output875×515 63.2 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/a/a268ba7222508996cbf82d1d5c9f80568e7330ac.jpeg "Example PVP matches output")

# Weekly Digest - Page 4 - Summaries - Talk.Markets

[Weekly Digest](https://talk.markets/t/weekly-digest/1742)

===========================================================

[Summaries](https://talk.markets/c/summaries/67)

[digest](https://talk.markets/tag/digest)

[Yor](https://talk.markets/u/Yor)
 (Yor Forger) 21 December 2025 07:00 153

[](https://talk.markets/t/weekly-digest/1742?page=4#p-21606-weekly-forum-activity-report-1)
Weekly Forum Activity Report
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**TLDR**: Over the past week, the forum witnessed vibrant discussions focusing on cryptocurrency market stability, the promise of altcoins and novel blockchain technologies, while fascinating insights were shared on how different monetary policies are shaping market dynamics.

[](https://talk.markets/t/weekly-digest/1742?page=4#p-21606-feed-2)
[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69)

===========================================================================================================

*   ![:money_bag:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/money_bag.png?v=15 ":money_bag:") [**Payments in the Agentic Economy**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8111/1)
    : Discussions around how autonomous agents conduct transactions highlighted trust and infrastructure needs for stablecoin payments.
*   ![:coin:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/coin.png?v=15 ":coin:") [**Bitcoin Is Building a Base as ETF Flows Stabilize**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8110/1)
    : Bitcoin’s market dynamics with ETF flows balancing were critically analyzed, despite weak demand and unreliable inflation data.
*   ![:dollar_banknote:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/dollar_banknote.png?v=15 ":dollar_banknote:") [**Love Language**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8109/1)
    : Arthur Hayes delves into the impacts of QE and RMP on inflation, emphasizing significant repercussions for financial markets.
*   ![:magnifying_glass_tilted_left:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/magnifying_glass_tilted_left.png?v=15 ":magnifying_glass_tilted_left:") [**Introducing: Taker-Flow-Based Gamma Exposure**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8108/1)
    : New metrics on crypto market volatility through dealer hedging impacts offer traders enhanced strategies.
*   ![:globe_showing_europe_africa:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/globe_showing_europe_africa.png?v=15 ":globe_showing_europe_africa:") [**Let a thousand societies bloom**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8107/1)
    : Vitalik Buterin’s vision of diverse societal affiliations proposes innovation through cultural evolution.
*   ![:chart_decreasing:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/chart_decreasing.png?v=15 ":chart_decreasing:") [**Trapped Under Overhead Supply**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8106/1)
    : Bitcoin remains pressured by dense overhead supply, impacting market recovery efforts.
*   ![:link:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/link.png?v=15 ":link:") [**Bitcoin In A Fragile Flow Regime**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8105/1)
    : BTC’s price impact from ETF flows highlights ongoing stabilization with little directional movement expected.
*   ![:chart_increasing:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/chart_increasing.png?v=15 ":chart_increasing:") [**The Altcoin Vector #33**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8104/1)
    : The report identifies significant trading opportunities in the altcoin markets via Glassnode insights.
*   ![:bar_chart:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/bar_chart.png?v=15 ":bar_chart:") [**The Bitcoin Vector #34**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8103/1)
    : Market insights require a paid subscription, offering exclusive analysis on Bitcoin trends by Swissblock.
*   ![:light_bulb:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/light_bulb.png?v=15 ":light_bulb:") [**Bad Market. One Obvious Bet: $EDEL**](https://talk.markets/t/-/8100/1)
    : An exploration of $EDEL as a promising investment in tough market conditions highlights its strategic catalysts.

The discussions provided unembellished insights into the evolving crypto landscape, equipping forum members with data-driven perspectives and market strategies.

[Yor](https://talk.markets/u/Yor)
 (Yor Forger) 28 December 2025 07:00 154

[](https://talk.markets/t/weekly-digest/1742?page=4#p-21642-tldr-1)
TLDR
------------------------------------------------------------------------

During the week of December 21 to December 28, 2025, key discussions in the forum centered on trends and analyses within the cryptocurrency market, particularly revolving around Bitcoin and altcoins. Critical insights were shared on the lack of sustained inflows into Bitcoin ETFs, stagnation within the DeFi sector, and the broader economic implications reflected in current market structures. Additionally, the condition of Bitcoin’s macroeconomic environment was evaluated, suggesting a potential future recovery.

[](https://talk.markets/t/weekly-digest/1742?page=4#p-21642-feed-2)
[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69)

===========================================================================================================

*   ![:chart_decreasing:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/chart_decreasing.png?v=15 ":chart_decreasing:") [Bitcoin ETFs Lack a Sustained Inflow Streak](https://talk.markets/t/-/8129/2)
    : The article underscores the lack of consistent ETF inflow as a sign of market stabilization, rather than recovery, and advises caution.
*   ![:globe_with_meridians:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/globe_with_meridians.png?v=15 ":globe_with_meridians:") [The Stagnation](https://talk.markets/t/-/8128/2)
    : Analyzes the reasons behind the stagnation in DeFi’s Total Value Locked, highlighting significant declines from previous cycles.
*   ![:christmas_tree:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/christmas_tree.png?v=15 ":christmas_tree:") [Signing out for 2025](https://talk.markets/t/-/8122/2)
    : The Decentralised team reflects on 2025’s content as they break for the holidays, noting plans for future expansion.
*   ![:warning:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/warning.png?v=15 ":warning:") [Late-Cycle Signals Are Flashing Caution for Bitcoin](https://talk.markets/t/-/8121/2)
    : Discusses potential risks for Bitcoin as momentum indicators show signs of caution.

# Bitcoin Market Monitor - January 2026 - Feed - Talk.Markets

[Bitcoin Market Monitor - January 2026](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-market-monitor-january-2026/8154)

=========================================================================================================

[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69)

[ecoinometrics-substack-com](https://talk.markets/tag/ecoinometrics-substack-com)

[Wolf](https://talk.markets/u/Wolf)   4 January 2026 14:41 1

[@Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/sakura)
 please summarize this article, thanks uwu.

[Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/Sakura)
 (Sakura) 4 January 2026 14:41 2

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-market-monitor-january-2026/8154#p-21688-tldr-1)
TLDR:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The January 2026 Bitcoin Market Monitor indicates a stabilization in the market, but Bitcoin is currently in a consolidation phase rather than a recovery.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-market-monitor-january-2026/8154#p-21688-key-points-2)
Key Points:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   ![:chart_decreasing:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/chart_decreasing.png?v=15 ":chart_decreasing:") Bitcoin has underperformed compared to other assets, ending 2025 with negative returns.
*   ![:bar_chart:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/bar_chart.png?v=15 ":bar_chart:") Macro conditions are improving slightly, but not enough to support a strong recovery.
*   ![:counterclockwise_arrows_button:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/counterclockwise_arrows_button.png?v=15 ":counterclockwise_arrows_button:") ETF flows have stabilized but remain below zero, indicating indecision in the market.
*   ![:balance_scale:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/balance_scale.png?v=15 ":balance_scale:") Bitcoin’s price stability is expected, with caution advised for rallies without flow support.
*   ![:magnifying_glass_tilted_left:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/magnifying_glass_tilted_left.png?v=15 ":magnifying_glass_tilted_left:") The next phase for Bitcoin will depend on market flows rather than narratives.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-market-monitor-january-2026/8154#p-21688-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth summary:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Bitcoin Market Monitor** for January 2026 provides a detailed analysis of Bitcoin’s current market position, focusing on liquidity trends, ETF flows, and macroeconomic signals. The report highlights that while the market has stabilized, Bitcoin has lost its leadership position, finishing 2025 as a laggard with negative returns. This underperformance is not reflected in the broader risk market, where equities and gold have shown resilience, suggesting that Bitcoin’s struggles are more specific to its own dynamics rather than a general market downturn.

The macro environment has seen some improvement, particularly with easing U.S. financial conditions, but these changes have not yet translated into supportive conditions for Bitcoin. The report notes that while ETF outflows have slowed and liquidation pressures have eased, Bitcoin is still trading at a significant discount compared to its implied fair value based on Nasdaq performance. This indicates a complex interplay between Bitcoin’s internal mechanics and broader market sentiment.

Looking ahead, the report emphasizes that Bitcoin is currently in a consolidation phase rather than a rebound. The stabilization of ETF flows suggests that immediate downside risks have diminished, but the potential for upward movement is limited without strong capital rotation. The analysis concludes that Bitcoin’s future trajectory will be determined by market flows, highlighting the importance of cautious [optimism](https://talk.markets/t/233?silent=true)
 in the current environment.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-market-monitor-january-2026/8154#p-21688-eli5-4)
ELI5:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The January 2026 Bitcoin Market Monitor says that Bitcoin’s price is not doing great right now. It has been going down and is not leading the market like it used to. The overall market is getting a little better, but Bitcoin is still stuck. People are unsure about buying more Bitcoin, so its price is stable but not really going up. The report suggests being careful with any price increases unless there’s strong support from investors.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-market-monitor-january-2026/8154#p-21688-writers-main-point-5)
Writers main point:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The primary point of the article is that Bitcoin is in a consolidation phase, with market flows determining its future direction rather than optimistic narratives.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-market-monitor-january-2026/8154#p-21688-relevant-links-6)
Relevant links:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Ecoinometrics Substack](https://substack.com/@ecoinometrics)

# Learn to use Rick on Telegram - Rick Bot - Talk.Markets

[Learn to use Rick on Telegram](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306)

===========================================================================================

[Rick Bot](https://talk.markets/c/rick/61)

[telegram](https://talk.markets/tag/telegram)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)  24 November 2023 00:47 1

Did you know it’s possible to turn the contract responder off and there’s a very easy way to fix wrong tokens showing up?

Most of these things are documented briefly [somewhere](https://talk.markets/t/telegram-docs-rick-sanchez/1107)
, but I wanted to do a quick overview of the most common fixes for common problems, as well as just give some tips on how to use Rick.

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-wrong-token-is-showing-1)
Wrong token is showing
====================================================================================================================

You can do two things.

1.  Use `/z pepe 2` or `3` to get the next result (works with any query).
2.  Set a token filter for your group (any member can do this): `/rickfix pepe 0x...`

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-deleting-a-rick-message-2)
Deleting a Rick message
======================================================================================================================

Just reply with `X` to any Rick message within a minute to delete it. “X” can either be upper or lowercase. _If you prefer this method, you can even use it to delete a message of your own!_

If /**buttons** are enabled you can also click the ![:cross_mark:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/cross_mark.png?v=15 ":cross_mark:") emoji where available.

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-do-not-respond-to-contracts-3)
Do not respond to contracts
==============================================================================================================================

Use `/autoresponder off` to prevent the bot from responding to contracts and chart links. As a result, pricebot will not show up anymore, but it can still be used by querying with `/z` or `/x`.

Use `/noresultmode off` to only have the bot respond if there is an active trading pair.

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-fix-twitter-previews-4)
Fix Twitter/𝕏 Previews
===================================================================================================================

See: [Better Twitter/X previews](https://talk.markets/t/better-twitter-x-embeds/1849)

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-check-socials-eth-sol-5)
Check socials (ETH + SOL)
======================================================================================================================

See: [Social Finder](https://talk.markets/t/social-finder/3445)

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-ignore-cashtags-6)
Ignore cashtags
======================================================================================================

If you want to prevent a response on $cashtags, you can turn this feature off with `/cashtags off`.

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-pricemode-7)
Pricemode
==========================================================================================

You can switch the default pricemode for the autoresponder and $cashtag responder with `pricemode sim` or `adv`.

The default mode (**adv**) will show a detailed price embed when you paste a contract. This is similar to using `/x`. You can try the difference quickly by running `/z pepe` and `/x pepe`.

By design, /z is meant to be used for a quick price check; it will show a minimalistic embed with compact information and keep your chat clean. You can default to this view by running `/pricemode sim` (for simple).

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-index-top-10-by-mcap-8)
Index (top 10 by mcap)
==================================================================================================================

See: [Index: Top coins by market cap](https://talk.markets/t/new-index-command-explained/2381)

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-coingecko-tokens-9)
CoinGecko tokens
========================================================================================================

For non-DEX tokens, you can use `/a doge` to query information from CoinGecko. To get the next result, use `/a doge 2`.

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-quick-x-project-info-10)
Quick X Project info
=================================================================================================================

Use `/moni blur_io` to get a quick scan of any Twitter/𝕏/X account. This data is available in full on [Moni Discover](https://discover.getmoni.io/?ref=HZMJHX)
.

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-reminders-11)
Reminders
===========================================================================================

Set quick reminders for anything. See: [Using reminders](https://talk.markets/t/using-reminders/3475)

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-alpha-pings-12)
Alpha Pings
===============================================================================================

Since [@everyone](https://talk.markets/groups/everyone)
 is not a feature in Telegram, we can use pins to ping all members. Only admins can use this command. Having a title is sufficient. There are three ways to use this.

*   Just send `/ping`.
*   Reply with `/ping` to a message.
*   Send `/ping <message here>`.

Just try them out and see the difference in execution for yourself.

> \[!notice\] Rick needs pin permissions for the remind/ping features to be effective.

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-ai-credits-13)
AI credits
=============================================================================================

> \[!rick\] Learn about [credits](https://talk.markets/t/credits-rick-sanchez/1136)
> ; they are used for AI commands. If your group is using Rick, it’s likely you already have some AI credits.

[](https://talk.markets/t/learn-to-use-rick-on-telegram/1306#p-6484-wubba-ping-check-14)
Wubba (ping check)
===========================================================================================================

Type /wubba for a simple response check. You can use this to check if the bot is responsive. A successful response should say: “Burp… Ping! That took about… **113ms**.” You may also check /status to check if services are up and running.

[Commands on Telegram](https://talk.markets/t/commands-on-telegram/1465)

[New Trendings, Favorites & Better Reminders](https://talk.markets/t/new-trendings-favorites-better-reminders/5711)

[\[2024\] Telegram updates for Rick](https://talk.markets/t/2024-telegram-updates-for-rick/1155/12)

[Starting with Rick](https://talk.markets/t/starting-with-rick/1135)

# Arbitrum One :arbi: [cheatsheet] - Chains - Talk.Markets

[Arbitrum One :arbi: \[cheatsheet\]](https://talk.markets/t/arbitrum-one-cheatsheet/173)

=========================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Chains](https://talk.markets/c/guides/chains/39)

[cheatsheet](https://talk.markets/tag/cheatsheet)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   1 September 2021 17:08 1

Arbitrum One is a L2 (Layer 2) network on the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Mainnet (this is a Layer 1 solution). It allows cheaper transactions then you’d see on the L1 mainnet. Scroll to the bottom for some more articles about Arbitrum.

[](https://talk.markets/t/arbitrum-one-cheatsheet/173#p-258-network-details-1)
Network Details
==============================================================================================

*   **Network Name**: Arbitrum
*   **RPC**: [https://arb1.arbitrum.io/rpc](https://arb1.arbitrum.io/rpc)
    
*   ****Chain ID**: 42161**
*   **Currency Symbol**: ETH
*   **Block Explorer URL**: [https://arbiscan.io/](https://arbiscan.io/)
    

> **TIP:** You can add network easily, search **Arbitrum One** on [Chainlist](https://chainlist.org/chain/42161)

# Bitcoin’s Multi-Year Outperformance Streak Has Stalled - Feed - Talk.Markets

[Bitcoin’s Multi-Year Outperformance Streak Has Stalled](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-s-multi-year-outperformance-streak-has-stalled/8150)

=============================================================================================================================================

[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69)

[ecoinometrics-substack-com](https://talk.markets/tag/ecoinometrics-substack-com)

[Wolf](https://talk.markets/u/Wolf)   2 January 2026 13:43 1

[@Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/sakura)
 please summarize this article, thanks uwu.

[Weekly Digest](https://talk.markets/t/weekly-digest/1742/155)

[Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/Sakura)
 (Sakura) 2 January 2026 13:43 2

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-s-multi-year-outperformance-streak-has-stalled/8150#p-21678-tldr-1)
TLDR:
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bitcoin’s performance has stalled, diverging from other assets, while 2025 marked its least volatile year in a decade. ![:glowing_star:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/glowing_star.png?v=15 ":glowing_star:")

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-s-multi-year-outperformance-streak-has-stalled/8150#p-21678-key-points-2)
Key Points:
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   ![:chart_decreasing:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/chart_decreasing.png?v=15 ":chart_decreasing:") Bitcoin is down about 6% over the past year, while gold has surged over 60%.
*   ![:bar_chart:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/bar_chart.png?v=15 ":bar_chart:") 2025 was Bitcoin’s least volatile year, indicating a shift in market behavior.
*   ![:bank:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/bank.png?v=15 ":bank:") The Federal Reserve has stopped shrinking its balance sheet, which may support financial conditions.
*   ![:magnifying_glass_tilted_left:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/magnifying_glass_tilted_left.png?v=15 ":magnifying_glass_tilted_left:") Current market conditions are mixed, with Bitcoin’s weakness appearing isolated rather than systemic.
*   ![:hourglass_not_done:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/hourglass_not_done.png?v=15 ":hourglass_not_done:") The focus for early 2026 will be on demand recovery rather than macro policy changes.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-s-multi-year-outperformance-streak-has-stalled/8150#p-21678-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth summary:
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article discusses the recent performance of Bitcoin, highlighting that its multi-year outperformance streak has come to a halt. Over the past year, Bitcoin has seen a decline of approximately 6%, contrasting sharply with gold’s impressive gain of over 60%. This divergence is significant as it suggests that Bitcoin’s struggles are not part of a broader market downturn, as many other risk-on assets, like the Nasdaq 100 and S&P 500, continue to show positive returns. The article emphasizes that Bitcoin’s current weakness seems to be more idiosyncratic, likely linked to position unwinds and a lack of demand recovery.

Additionally, 2025 has been noted as Bitcoin’s least volatile year in the past decade, which is a notable shift given the increasing role of institutional capital in the market. This lower volatility indicates that Bitcoin is behaving more like a mature macro asset rather than a high-risk momentum trade. The article also touches on the Federal Reserve’s recent actions, stating that while the balance sheet has been reduced significantly, the active phase of contraction is over, which may provide a more stable macro backdrop for Bitcoin.

Looking ahead, the article suggests that the key to Bitcoin’s recovery lies in the return of demand as we enter Q1 2026. The current market conditions are not overtly hostile, but they lack clear demand confirmation, making it essential for investors to remain patient and observant of market flows rather than rushing into trades.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-s-multi-year-outperformance-streak-has-stalled/8150#p-21678-eli5-4)
ELI5:
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bitcoin has not been doing well lately, losing value while gold has been doing great. Last year was the calmest for Bitcoin, meaning its price didn’t change much. The people in charge of money (the Federal Reserve) have stopped taking money out of the system, which might help Bitcoin. Now, everyone is waiting to see if more people will want to buy Bitcoin again.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-s-multi-year-outperformance-streak-has-stalled/8150#p-21678-writers-main-point-5)
Writers main point:
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The author argues that while Bitcoin’s performance has stalled and is currently isolated from broader market trends, the conditions are not entirely negative, and the focus should be on whether demand will return in early 2026.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-s-multi-year-outperformance-streak-has-stalled/8150#p-21678-relevant-links-6)

# You can be right and still lose if you’re early - Feed - Talk.Markets

[You can be right and still lose if you’re early](https://talk.markets/t/you-can-be-right-and-still-lose-if-you-re-early/8149)

===============================================================================================================================

[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69)

[threadingontheedge-substack-com](https://talk.markets/tag/threadingontheedge-substack-com)

[Wolf](https://talk.markets/u/Wolf)   2 January 2026 13:07 1

[@Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/sakura)
 please summarize this article, thanks uwu.

[Weekly Digest](https://talk.markets/t/weekly-digest/1742/155)

[Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/Sakura)
 (Sakura) 2 January 2026 13:07 2

[](https://talk.markets/t/you-can-be-right-and-still-lose-if-you-re-early/8149#p-21676-tldr-1)
TLDR:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In 2025, being right about crypto investments didn’t guarantee success due to timing issues, fragile market conditions, and the need for mental resilience.

[](https://talk.markets/t/you-can-be-right-and-still-lose-if-you-re-early/8149#p-21676-key-points-2)
Key Points:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   ![:hourglass_not_done:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/hourglass_not_done.png?v=15 ":hourglass_not_done:") **Time vs. Price**: The real challenge in 2025 was time, not just price movements.
*   ![:chart_decreasing:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/chart_decreasing.png?v=15 ":chart_decreasing:") **Valuations vs. Users**: High valuations with low user engagement are red flags.
*   ![:brain:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/brain.png?v=15 ":brain:") **Mental Resilience**: Staying rational amidst market chaos is crucial for investors.
*   ![:locked:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/locked.png?v=15 ":locked:") **Security Matters**: Security is now a fundamental part of product development in crypto.
*   ![:balance_scale:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/balance_scale.png?v=15 ":balance_scale:") **Leverage Risks**: Using leverage can amplify mistakes more than it can enhance gains.

[](https://talk.markets/t/you-can-be-right-and-still-lose-if-you-re-early/8149#p-21676-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth summary:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article reflects on the tumultuous year of 2025 in the crypto market, emphasizing that the primary challenge was not just the fluctuating prices but the critical element of time. Many projects struggled to prove their viability as the market shifted rapidly, exposing vulnerabilities in their financial structures and user engagement. The author notes that while trading allows for quick decisions, venture capital in crypto often locks investors into long-term commitments, making survival a more pressing concern than immediate returns.

The piece also highlights the alarming trend of projects achieving high valuations despite having minimal user engagement, which signals potential instability. The author warns that such valuations often mask underlying issues, as they are frequently driven by temporary incentives rather than genuine product-market fit. As the market evolves, the focus is shifting from story-based pricing to a more rigorous evaluation of unit economics and user retention.

Finally, the article stresses the importance of mental resilience for investors, as the crypto market can be psychologically taxing. It suggests that having a clear investment strategy and understanding the security landscape is essential for navigating future challenges. The author concludes with a call to action for investors to adapt to these lessons as they move into 2026.

[](https://talk.markets/t/you-can-be-right-and-still-lose-if-you-re-early/8149#p-21676-eli5-4)
ELI5:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In 2025, many people thought they were making smart choices in crypto, but they were too early, and that hurt them. Just because a project looks good on paper doesn’t mean it has real users. Investors need to stay calm and think clearly, even when the market is crazy. Also, keeping things safe is super important now, and using too much borrowed money can lead to big mistakes.

[](https://talk.markets/t/you-can-be-right-and-still-lose-if-you-re-early/8149#p-21676-writers-main-point-5)
Writers main point:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main point is that in the crypto world, being right about a project doesn’t guarantee success if you’re too early; understanding time, user engagement, and maintaining mental resilience are key to thriving in this volatile market.

[](https://talk.markets/t/you-can-be-right-and-still-lose-if-you-re-early/8149#p-21676-relevant-links-6)
Relevant links:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TLDR:

The article outlines 0xKyle’s investment strategy and predictions for 2026, emphasizing a shift from crypto to equities and the growing influence of retail investors. ![:glowing_star:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/glowing_star.png?v=15 ":glowing_star:")

[](https://talk.markets/t/the-2026-gameplan/8151#p-21680-key-points-2)
Key Points:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Investment Strategy**: Focus on trend-following and asset picking, with a preference for average returns. ![:chart_increasing:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/chart_increasing.png?v=15 ":chart_increasing:")
*   **Market Outlook**: Crypto is in a bear market, and equities are becoming more appealing due to increased retail participation. ![:chart_decreasing:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/chart_decreasing.png?v=15 ":chart_decreasing:")
*   **Retail Investing Growth**: Retail investors are entering the market at unprecedented levels, impacting traditional market structures. ![:globe_showing_europe_africa:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/globe_showing_europe_africa.png?v=15 ":globe_showing_europe_africa:")
*   **Predictions for 2026**: Expect significant movements in gold, robotics, and stablecoins, while crypto may continue to struggle. ![:crystal_ball:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/crystal_ball.png?v=15 ":crystal_ball:")

[](https://talk.markets/t/the-2026-gameplan/8151#p-21680-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth summary:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In his annual memo, 0xKyle reflects on the evolution of the crypto market over the past four years, noting significant changes in Bitcoin’s price and the overall market sentiment. He emphasizes his straightforward investment strategy, which revolves around trend-following during bull markets and careful asset selection. This approach has allowed him to maintain a steady performance while enjoying a balanced lifestyle, even amidst a challenging year for crypto, where many assets have seen negative returns.

Looking ahead to 2026, Kyle predicts that the crypto market will remain volatile and bear-like, with traders needing to adapt their strategies. He highlights the increasing role of retail investors, who are now participating in the market at levels comparable to the pandemic peak. This democratization of investing is shifting traditional market dynamics, making equities more attractive compared to speculative crypto assets. Kyle suggests that retail investors are likely to gravitate towards more stable and fundamentally sound investments.

Kyle also shares his predictions for 2026, including a bullish outlook on gold and robotics, while expressing skepticism about the future of many cryptocurrencies. He believes that adapting to the evolving market landscape is crucial for success, urging investors to embrace flexibility and broaden their investment horizons. Ultimately, he concludes that the key to thriving in the current environment is to adapt or risk falling behind.

# Introducing Skills - Features - Talk.Markets

[Introducing Skills](https://talk.markets/t/introducing-skills/8068)

=====================================================================

[Rick Bot](https://talk.markets/c/rick/61) [Features](https://talk.markets/c/rick/features/71)

[telegram](https://talk.markets/tag/telegram)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   4 December 2025 07:00 1

**December became known for shipping a fun feature!** Skills allow you to slowly progress your profile while doing what you always do - being active on Telegram. Simply run the `/me` command to see your current progress and levels.

[![image](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/2X/d/d03d07db8e8e35284490789d724627b1954a8200_2_1380x774.jpeg)\
\
image1848×1039 134 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/d/d03d07db8e8e35284490789d724627b1954a8200.jpeg "image")

[](https://talk.markets/t/introducing-skills/8068#p-21527-how-does-it-work-1)
How does it work?
===============================================================================================

Run `/me` to see your current levels and rankings.

As you are active, you will receive XP in various skills, there are 12 skills in total, meaning the total level you could eventually reach is **1188** (`12*99`). _**You can only check your own stats.**_

[](https://talk.markets/t/introducing-skills/8068#p-21527-skills-2)
Skills
==========================================================================

**Aura ![:brain:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/brain.png?v=15 ":brain:")**   
XP is given on any activity.

**Providing ![:handshake:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/handshake.png?v=15 ":handshake:")**   
XP is given based on `#UPDATE` alerts in your name. _Premium skill, because only [premium groups](https://talk.markets/t/learn-about-rick-premium/1021)
 receive these alerts consistently._

**Bonding ![:counterclockwise_arrows_button:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/counterclockwise_arrows_button.png?v=15 ":counterclockwise_arrows_button:")**   
XP is given when you scanned a token that bonds. _[Migration alerts must be active in your group.](https://talk.markets/t/migration-reminders/5401)
_

**Degening ![:slot_machine:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/slot_machine.png?v=15 ":slot_machine:"), Trading ![:chart_increasing:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/chart_increasing.png?v=15 ":chart_increasing:") and Whaling ![:whale:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/whale.png?v=15 ":whale:")**   
XP is given for sub 100k, sub 1M and 1M+ FDV scans.

**Prompting ![:robot:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/robot.png?v=15 ":robot:")**   
XP is given on AI interactions.

**Shitposting ![:speech_balloon:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/speech_balloon.png?v=15 ":speech_balloon:")**   
XP is given on any text activity.

**Memery ![:performing_arts:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/performing_arts.png?v=15 ":performing_arts:")**   
XP is given on sticker/GIF usage.

**Whispering ![:love_letter:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/love_letter.png?v=15 ":love_letter:")**   
XP is given when privately using Rick.

**Governance ![:ballot_box_with_ballot:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/ballot_box_with_ballot.png?v=15 ":ballot_box_with_ballot:")**   
XP is given when using the [Reputation System](https://talk.markets/t/new-reputation-system/7117)
.

**Researching ![:books:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/books.png?v=15 ":books:")**   
XP is given on long texts or sharing web & Twitter/𝕏 links.

**Doomscrolling ![:mobile_phone_with_arrow:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/mobile_phone_with_arrow.png?v=15 ":mobile_phone_with_arrow:")**   
XP is given upon sharing social media links.

**Botmastery ![:laptop:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/laptop.png?v=15 ":laptop:")**   
XP is given when using /commands.

[](https://talk.markets/t/introducing-skills/8068#p-21527-faq-3)
FAQ
====================================================================

**Will there be leaderboards?**  
Your **rank** is shown if you are within the **top 1000** of a skill. Your name will never be visible on public boards.

> \[!warning\] Keep in mind, if you are **using automations** with Rick, you do have a chance to get a [permanent ban](https://talk.markets/t/ratelimits/5982)
>  from using Rick.

The regulators are rolling out a comprehensive roadmap that aims to create a structured environment for crypto operations. This initiative is part of a broader strategy to integrate Hong Kong into the international crypto ecosystem, making it a more attractive destination for investors and businesses alike.

By prioritizing global liquidity, Hong Kong aims to foster a more robust and interconnected market. The roadmap is expected to provide clear guidelines and regulations that will help build investor confidence, encouraging more participation in the crypto space. This strategic move could potentially position Hong Kong as a leading hub for cryptocurrency activities, attracting both local and international players.

Overall, the article highlights the proactive steps being taken by Hong Kong regulators to ensure that the region remains competitive in the rapidly evolving world of cryptocurrency. The focus on global liquidity and a structured regulatory framework is seen as essential for the future growth and stability of the crypto market in Hong Kong.

# Clan Rankings 🎖️ - Features - Talk.Markets

[Clan Rankings 🎖️](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134)

===============================================================

[Rick Bot](https://talk.markets/c/rick/61) [Features](https://talk.markets/c/rick/features/71)

[telegram](https://talk.markets/tag/telegram)
, [clans](https://talk.markets/tag/clans)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   28 December 2024 09:09 1

A fun and competitive way to compare your [clan](https://talk.markets/t/-/2656)
 with other clans! **Clan Rankings** with Rick give XP and let you level up your group, enabling various leaderboards based on plays shared within the clan!

> \[!new\] Keep in mind that this is a rolling leaderboard, during the first days of each new week/month rankings are updated **as you claim your XP.** They will get more accurate towards the end of the week/month.

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-related-commands-1)
Related commands
=========================================================================================

> \[!note\] XP is not given if /rank is not called. The most active groups claim every day. **After 3 days, XP given is reduced.**

*   `/rank` - claim XP **every day** and check common stats
*   `/rank league` or `/rank lg` - view leaderboards within your current league
*   `/rank rankname` - view league leaderboard for specific rank
*   `/clantag` - to manage your [clantag](https://talk.markets/t/-/2656)
    

> \[!tip\] Use /**setsocial** to have your clantag link to your group’s Twitter/𝕏 on the leaderboards.

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-fireworks-wrapped-2)
![:fireworks:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/fireworks.png?v=15 ":fireworks:") Wrapped
============================================================================================================================================================================

Starting from 2026-01-08T00:00:00Z, a **wrapped** leaderboard will be generated. To access it, simply run the command `/rank`. You can view the top 25 rankings as well as your own current position by using the `/wrapped` command.

> \[!warning\] _After getting your Wrapped XP, run `/rank` again to claim your daily XP._

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-leagues-3)
Leagues
=======================================================================

The `/rank league` command (abbreviated as `/rank lg`) displays a leaderboard exclusively featuring clans that belong to the same league as your own. Leagues are designed to ensure an enjoyable experience for all clans.

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-ranks-and-emojis-4)
Ranks and Emojis
=========================================================================================

The current ranks (leagues) and their associated emoji’s. You can view any ranked leaderboard with `/rank rankname`, use `/rank lg` to view clans within your own league.

*   **Unranked** ![:seedling:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/seedling.png?v=15 ":seedling:")
*   **Bronze** ![:3rd_place_medal:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/3rd_place_medal.png?v=15 ":3rd_place_medal:")
*   **Silver** ![:2nd_place_medal:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/2nd_place_medal.png?v=15 ":2nd_place_medal:")
*   **Gold** ![:1st_place_medal:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/1st_place_medal.png?v=15 ":1st_place_medal:")
*   **Platinum** ![:military_medal:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/military_medal.png?v=15 ":military_medal:")
*   **Diamond** ![:gem_stone:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/gem_stone.png?v=15 ":gem_stone:")
*   **Master** ![:graduation_cap:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/graduation_cap.png?v=15 ":graduation_cap:")
*   **Grandmaster** ![:crown:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/crown.png?v=15 ":crown:")
*   **Challenger** ![:fire:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/fire.png?v=15 ":fire:")

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-preview-5)
Preview
=======================================================================

XP & the clan level are shown for various timeframes. Several real-time leaderboards are shown.

[![XP overview & level](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/9/97db26b44e96befdb98cf60cc7975f0ba1b7e512.jpeg)\
\
XP overview & level422×422 31 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/9/97db26b44e96befdb98cf60cc7975f0ba1b7e512.jpeg "XP overview & level")

  

[![Example of a monthly leaderboard](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/2X/7/7813914b555f67a2ccaee31f78a583b466dcb244_2_498x498.jpeg)\
\
Example of a monthly leaderboard666×666 52.8 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/7/7813914b555f67a2ccaee31f78a583b466dcb244.jpeg "Example of a monthly leaderboard")

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-rules-6)
Rules
===================================================================

1.  All chats participating must configure a [clantag](https://talk.markets/t/-/2656)
    .
2.  You can claim your XP **every day** (24 hours) - _best XP potential!_
3.  You should at least claim every 72 hours.
4.  After 72 hours, a slight penalty is added to the XP received.
5.  There are currently **no rewards** in any form; do not get scammed.

> \[!warning\] Bots will be banned from clans, I have nothing against some bots and autoforwarders that trigger Rick and help you in the trenches, but it’s unfair. If you want to participate, use a separate chat with your auto-scan/signal bots. If you feel the ban is incorrect, [please reach out](https://talk.markets/t/contact-feedback-socials/1143)
> .

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-faq-7)
FAQ
===============================================================

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-how-does-my-clan-get-xp-8)
How does my clan get XP?
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The primary way to earn XP is by **sharing good plays** and **being active** within the group; your [ATH leaderboards](https://talk.markets/t/ath-leaderboards/3111)
 are a good insight into how your group performs.

Specific details will remain undisclosed to minimise the potential for abuse and cheating. Ultimately, the aim is to ensure a **fair** and **competitive** environment on the clan leaderboards.

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-level-unlocking-why-9)
“Level: Unlocking..” Why?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Just keep claiming daily; when your clan reaches 100%, you will see your level.

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-what-does-next-daily-mean-10)
What does “Next daily” mean?
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the footer, you will always see the remaining time until your next claim. Ideally, **it is best to run the rank command daily**; however, running it every 2-3 days is also acceptable, albeit with a slight disadvantage in terms of experience points (XP). **Skip longer then 3 days, and XP awarded is nerved massively.**

This basically means these leaderboards are always dynamic, resulting in a fun experience no matter what rank you are!

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-how-to-interpret-these-rankings-11)
How to interpret these rankings?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It’s quite straightforward; allow 1 to 2 weeks for everything to crystallise, as many groups will be opting in and accruing initial experience points (XP). The leaderboards require some time to gather data and provide more meaningful insights.

[](https://talk.markets/t/clan-rankings/5134#p-16311-but-chats-that-scan-a-lot-will-always-get-more-xp-12)
But chats that scan a lot will always get more XP..
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Yes, generally this is true, XP is a formula based on **activity** AND **scan performance**. This is why there will be multiple leagues. You can run `/rank lg` (league) to see leaderboards that only include chats that are in the same league.

Keywords: proof of clan, clan rankings update, clanrank

# Yield Farming on BSC - Introduction - Crypto & DeFi - Talk.Markets

[Yield Farming on BSC - Introduction](https://talk.markets/t/yield-farming-on-bsc-introduction/38)

===================================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Crypto & DeFi](https://talk.markets/c/guides/crypto/16)

[yield-farming](https://talk.markets/tag/yield-farming)
, [cp](https://talk.markets/tag/cp)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)  22 March 2021 00:44 1

[](https://talk.markets/t/yield-farming-on-bsc-introduction/38#p-47-binance-smart-chain-high-yield-farming-1)
[Binance](https://accounts.binance.com/en/register?ref=VEURIJ5P)
 Smart Chain – High Yield Farming
================================================================================================================================================================================================================

BSC is very new & hyped, most projects are very young and 99% scams. This is considered very high risk, be prepared to lose money. We are early, it helps a lot. Diversify and don’t ape in only one shitcoin.

### [](https://talk.markets/t/yield-farming-on-bsc-introduction/38#p-47-bsc-binance-smart-chain-bep-20-2)
BSC = [Binance](https://accounts.binance.com/en/register?ref=VEURIJ5P)
 Smart Chain (BEP-20)

When making withdrawals to your BSC wallet, always remember to select the BSC network: BEP-20.

Wallet extensions:

*   MetaMask ([how to connect with BSC](https://talk.markets/t/network-details-for-metamask-bsc-binance-smart-chain/39)
    )
*   [Binance Chain Chrome Extension](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/binance-chain-wallet/fhbohimaelbohpjbbldcngcnapndodjp)
    
*   [EzDeFi](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/ezdefi/ejeemacpidnaejkhpbmfkadhgjhnolaa#:~:text=ezDeFi&text=EzDeFi%20is%20an%20extension%20for,50%2B%20assets%20on%20multiple%20blockchains.)
    

I have good experience with MetaMask on iOS also (you can sync with the browser extension). Use browser in MetaMask on mobile, not Safari.

Pools or farms?

Keeping it simple, from high to low risk.

*   1.  Farms > imo, the best you can do.
*   2.  Pools > safest option.
*   3.  HODL > incredibly stupid, just pool then.

**Farms provide liquidity.** It allows people to buy & sell.

Without people farming (liquidity pools) you can not buy or sell the tokens. This is considered the most high risk method of farming, since you exchange your “real” tokens (ex. BNB) for LP tokens (a smart contract). LP tokens can be rigged/rugpulled by the dev team. The lower the liquidity, the higher the APY, ofcourse this is to motivate people to provide liquidity.

If you want to farm 100 CAKE, you would have to provide liquidity on a 1:1 ratio for the farm you choose, so for 100 CAKE you would add approx. need another 6,5 BNB at the time of writing, to get your LP tokens.

BNB or BUSD farms?

This is pure choice of personal risk appetite. Impermanent loss is a key here. If you are in CAKE/BNB-LP and CAKE goes +50% and BNB -50% you would be break even when you exchange your LP tokens back (excluding your gained rewards). If you are in a BNB pool you will most likely have less price volatilty risk, choose your risk level appropiately. Just keep an eye on the liquidity. You can get out of the farm at any time, no locking period I have seen so far.

Since all BSC activity **needs** BNB, most people choose BNB farms because of the gain potential from BNB. This is also why APY for BUSD pools have lower APY returns. _Theoritical logic behind this is, as long as people keep earning (big) money on BSC, so keep using BSC (and constantly buying BNB and paying BNB fees) BNB has to go up!_

**Pooling is the simple staking as most of us know it.**

Reward and risk is lower than farms. There is no maturation period for most coins, so you get rewards as soon as you pool. There is less risk, no risk for rugpulls (well, you are exposed to the price, ofcourse). You can tokens take out at any time, or compound them.

**Don’t HODL your coins** too long or if you do, don’t overrisk.

Most (shit)projects give very high ROI, everyone at least stakes or farms and is profiting from this, deflating the price. You’re missing out and will probably lose, since there will be a lot of profit taking from people that do farm/pool.

[](https://talk.markets/t/yield-farming-on-bsc-introduction/38#p-47-related-links-3)
Related links
==================================================================================================

*   [URL list - Yield Optimizers (auto-compounding)](https://talk.markets/t/url-list-yield-optimizers-auto-compounding/95)

# Interesting facts/knowledge (off-topic) - General - Talk.Markets

# Solana Network :sol: [cheatsheet] - Chains - Talk.Markets

[Solana Network :sol: \[cheatsheet\]](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56)

===========================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Chains](https://talk.markets/c/guides/chains/39)

[solana](https://talk.markets/tag/solana)
, [cheatsheet](https://talk.markets/tag/cheatsheet)
, [l1](https://talk.markets/tag/l1)

[Harvey](https://talk.markets/u/Harvey)   3 June 2021 16:34 1

**[Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)
** ![:sol:](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/4/4871e9fc071dc845d033bcbc5807ddf0be63bbae.png?v=15 ":sol:") is a **Layer 1 blockchain** designed for high performance and low-cost transactions, using a unique **Proof of History (PoH)** combined with **Proof of Stake (PoS)**. It achieves speeds of up to 65,000 transactions per second, low latency, and minimal fees, making it ideal for decentralised applications (dApps) and decentralised finance (DeFi) services that require rapid, secure, and scalable solutions.

[](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56#p-73-wallet-1)
Wallet
============================================================================

To connect with the [Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)
 network, install the [Phantom extension](https://phantom.app/)
 and create a wallet. Remember, securely store your private key!

[Phantom](https://phantom.app/)
 wallet is the recommended wallet to use for [Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)
, however, SolFlare and MagicEden wallet are very popular choices as well!

**Other wallets**

*   [SolFlare](https://solflare.com/)
    
*   [MagicEden Wallet](https://wallet.magiceden.io/)
    
*   [Glow](https://glow.app/)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56#p-73-botssnipers-dart-2)
Bots/Snipers ![:dart:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/dart.png?v=15 ":dart:")
========================================================================================================================================================================

*   [Photon for Solana](https://photon-sol.tinyastro.io/@RickBurpBot)
     ![:fire:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/fire.png?v=15 ":fire:") fastest charts & trading terminal
*   [Axiom](https://axiom.trade/@rick)
     ![:new_button:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/new_button.png?v=15 ":new_button:")
*   [GMGN](https://gmgn.ai/?chain=sol&ref=LbosYDck)
    
*   [Trojan on Solana](https://t.me/paris_trojanbot?start=r-rickbot)
    
*   [Maestro](https://t.me/maestro?start=r-rickburpbot)
    
*   [BananaGun for Solana](https://t.me/BananaGun_bot?start=ref_rickburpbot)
    
*   [Bonk Bot](https://t.me/bonkbot_bot?start=ref_rickbot)
    
*   [Sol Trading Bot](https://t.me/SolanaTradingBot?start=yqC7cGy1T)
    
*   [MevX](https://mevx.io/@RickBot)
    
*   [BullX Neo](https://t.me/BullxNeoBot?start=access_9NLRTPEP0RV)
    
*   [Consortium Key](https://t.me/ConsortiumKeyBot?start=ref_RickBurpBot)
    
*   [Magnum Trade Bot](https://t.me/magnum_trade_bot?start=mkEJIWpy)
    
*   [PepeBoost](https://t.me/pepeboost_sol08_bot?start=ref_0xRick)
    

> \[!tip\] Use [the Solana Incinerator](https://sol-incinerator.com/)
>  to close old token accounts and get some SOL back!

[](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56#p-73-bridges-3)
Bridges
==============================================================================

*   [deBridge](https://app.debridge.finance/r/8692)
     - TIP ![:sunny:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/sunny.png?v=15 ":sunny:")
*   [ChangeNow](https://changenow.io/exchange?amount=1&from=eth&to=sol&link_id=41a7df272da9da)
    
*   [RocketX](https://app.rocketx.exchange/?ref=LOTOAD7E)
     - slower, but cheap
*   [FixedFloat](https://fixedfloat.com/?ref=7a291hna)
    
*   [AllBridge](https://app.allbridge.io/bridge?from=POL&to=SOL&asset=SOL)
    
*   [Portalbridge](https://www.portalbridge.com/#/transfer)
     (known as Wormhole)
*   More: [Bridges: transfer funds between chains in DeFi](https://talk.markets/t/bridges-transfer-funds-between-chains-in-defi/68)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56#p-73-funding-from-exchange-4)
Funding from exchange
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can fund your wallet by withdrawing [Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)
 (**$SOL**) from [Binance](https://accounts.binance.com/en/register?ref=VEURIJ5P)
 or any [other CEX](https://talk.markets/t/url-cheatsheet-crypto-exchanges/108)
.

[](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56#p-73-solana-dexs-5)
[Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)
 DEX’s
===========================================================================================================================================================

*   [Jupiter](https://jup.ag/swap/)
     - best aggregator
*   [Raydium Swap](https://raydium.io/swap/)
    
*   [Pump Fun](https://pump.fun/)
     - [with better filters](https://poomp.fun/)
    
*   [Orca](https://www.orca.so/)
    
*   [Step Finance](https://app.step.finance/#/swap)
     (you can unwrap SOL here)

[Harvey](https://talk.markets/u/Harvey)   7 June 2021 02:35 1

You can find farms on [rugdoc.io](http://rugdoc.io/)
 or [vfat.tools](http://vfat.tools/)

AMM’s / Liquidity Pools

*   [https://app.sushi.com/pool](https://app.sushi.com/pool)
    
*   [QuickSwap](https://quickswap.exchange/#/swap)
    

Auto-Yield Optimizers (a.k.a. autocompounding)

*   [Adamant Finance](https://adamant.finance/)
    
*   [Beefy for Polygon](https://polygon.beefy.finance/)
    
*   [Firebird](https://app.firebird.finance/)
    
*   More in [this topic.](https://talk.markets/t/url-list-yield-optimizers-auto-compounding/95)

[cp](https://talk.markets/tag/cp)

[Talk.Markets](https://talk.markets/u/Talk.Markets)  10 June 2021 14:54 1

[](https://talk.markets/t/monitor-your-defi-wallet-portfolio/69#p-92-check-your-wallet-1)
Check your wallet
===========================================================================================================

The following list are dApps that connect with your wallet and scans all your holdings, farms and vaults. This will get you a nice overview of your DeFi portfolio.

[](https://talk.markets/t/monitor-your-defi-wallet-portfolio/69#p-92-popular-2)
Popular
=======================================================================================

*   [Debank](https://debank.com/)
     ETH, BSC, xDAI, Polygon, FTM, HECO, OKExChain
*   [Zapper.fi](https://zapper.fi/)
     for ETH and BTC
*   [Moni Portfolio Tracker](https://getmoni.io/)
    
*   [Zerion](https://app.zerion.io/)
     for ETH
*   [Ape Board](https://apeboard.finance/dashboard)
     > Now [Nansen Portfolio](https://portfolio.nansen.ai/)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/monitor-your-defi-wallet-portfolio/69#p-92-more-3)
More
=================================================================================

> Might include dead links..

*   [Tin.network](https://tin.network/en/home)
    
*   [WalletNow](https://walletnow.net/)
     BSC
*   [YieldWatch](https://www.yieldwatch.net/)
     BSC
*   [GemProtocol](https://gemprotocol.io/)
     BSC

# Bridges: transfer funds between chains in DeFi - Crypto & DeFi - Talk.Markets

[Bridges: transfer funds between chains in DeFi](https://talk.markets/t/bridges-transfer-funds-between-chains-in-defi/68)

==========================================================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Crypto & DeFi](https://talk.markets/c/guides/crypto/16)

[cp](https://talk.markets/tag/cp)
, [cheatsheet](https://talk.markets/tag/cheatsheet)
, [bridge](https://talk.markets/tag/bridge)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   10 June 2021 14:24 1

Below is a list of bridges you can use, to transfer your funds from chain to chain. DYOR - this is just a collection. I have not used every [bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)
 out there.

Keep in mind that many bridges, are also listed in the [Guides > Chains](https://talk.markets/c/guides/chains/39)
 cheatsheets.

> List of aggregators [in this topic](https://talk.markets/t/bridges-in-defi-aggregators/380)

[](https://talk.markets/t/bridges-transfer-funds-between-chains-in-defi/68#p-91-popular-bridges-1)
Popular Bridges
==================================================================================================================

*   [**deBridge**](https://talk.markets/debridge)
     - **TIP**: farm airdrop! ![:gift:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/gift.png?v=15 ":gift:")
*   [Rhino](https://app.rhino.fi/bridge)
    
*   [RocketX](https://app.rocketx.exchange/?ref=LOTOAD7E)
    
*   [Celer Bridge](https://cbridge.celer.network/#/transfer)
    
*   [Orbiter](https://www.orbiter.finance/?source=Ethereum&dest=Arbitrum)
    
*   [Synapse Protocol](https://synapseprotocol.com/)
    
*   [Across Protocol](https://across.to/?ref=0x310166751C19a2b1C37129a52ff8b433D8C6Df17)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/bridges-transfer-funds-between-chains-in-defi/68#p-91-more-bridges-2)
More bridges
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Symbiosis](https://app.symbiosis.finance/swap)
    
*   [Multichain](https://app.multichain.org/)
    
*   [xPollinate](https://www.xpollinate.io/)
    
*   [Transit](https://swap.transit.finance/#/)
    
*   [Wormhole (Portalbridge)](https://www.portalbridge.com/)
    
*   [LayerSwap](https://www.layerswap.io/)
    
*   [ChainHop](https://app.chainhop.exchange/?ref=0x310166751C19a2b1C37129a52ff8b433D8C6Df17)
    
*   [OwlTo Bridge](https://owlto.finance/rewards/?ref=0x310166751C19a2b1C37129a52ff8b433D8C6Df17)
     - supports testnets
*   [PolyNetwork](https://bridge.poly.network/)
    

TIP: If you need gas on any chain, check out: [How to get gas on any EVM chain?](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-get-gas-on-any-evm-chain/595)

> [![:light_bulb:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/light_bulb.png?v=15 ":light_bulb:")Check your DeFI wallet holdings + yield farms](https://talk.markets/t/check-your-defi-wallet-holdings-farms/69)

If you are too lazy to figure out your route, this spreadsheet might help - or [try an aggregator](https://talk.markets/t/bridges-in-defi-aggregators/380)
. I forgot who made it, he (or she) should probably add their Twitter/𝕏 @ in the sheets ![:grinning_face:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/grinning_face.png?v=15 ":grinning_face:") .

# BNB Chain (bsc) :bsc: [cheatsheet] - Chains - Talk.Markets

[BNB Chain (bsc) :bsc: \[cheatsheet\]](https://talk.markets/t/bnb-chain-bsc-cheatsheet/72)

===========================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Chains](https://talk.markets/c/guides/chains/39)

[cheatsheet](https://talk.markets/tag/cheatsheet)

[Talk.Markets](https://talk.markets/u/Talk.Markets)   10 June 2021 15:44 1

BNB Smart Chain is a high-performance blockchain platform designed to enable the development of scalable and user-friendly decentralized applications (DApps), particularly in the decentralized finance (DeFi) space.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bnb-chain-bsc-cheatsheet/72#p-96-setup-metamaskfunding-1)
Setup MetaMask/funding
==========================================================================================================

In Metamask go to Settings > Network and add the following information to get on BSC network.

You can fund your wallet by withdrawing **BNB** from [Binance](https://accounts.binance.com/en/register?ref=VEURIJ5P)
 to your MetaMask wallet address. If you want to [bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)
 from another chain, check out [bridges topic.](https://talk.markets/t/bridges-transfer-funds-between-chains-in-the-world-of-defi/68)

[](https://talk.markets/t/bnb-chain-bsc-cheatsheet/72#p-96-network-details-for-metamask-2)
Network Details for MetaMask
=======================================================================================================================

> ![:rocket:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/rocket.png?v=15 ":rocket:") Quickly add BNB Chain: go to [chainlist.org](http://chainlist.org/)
>  and search _**BSC**_. Full list of other RPC’s are also here.

*   **Network name**: BSC Mainnet
*   **RPC URL**: [https://bsc-dataseed.bnbchain.org](https://bsc-dataseed.bnbchain.org/)
    
*   **ChainID**: 56 _(if 56 doesn’t work, try `0x38`)_
*   **Symbol**: BNB
*   **Block Explorer**: `https://bscscan.com`

[](https://talk.markets/t/bnb-chain-bsc-cheatsheet/72#p-96-trading-bots-3)
Trading Bots
=======================================================================================

*   [Maestro](https://t.me/maestro?start=r-rickburpbot)
    
*   [BananaGun](https://t.me/BananaGunSniper_bot?start=ref_RickSanchez)
    
*   [Sigma](https://t.me/Sigma_buyBot?start=ref=450463357)
    
*   [Shuriken](https://t.me/ShurikenTradeBot?start=ref-MentionLux)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/bnb-chain-bsc-cheatsheet/72#p-96-bridge-4)
[Bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)

=====================================================================================================================

*   [Official BNB Bridge](https://www.bnbchain.org/en/bnb-chain-bridge)
    
*   [MEET48](https://gipr.meet48.com/#/bridge?noLogin=1)
    
*   [Pancakeswap](https://pancakeswap.finance/swap?outputCurrency=ETH&chainOut=eth)
    
*   [Debridge](https://app.debridge.com/?inputChain=1&outputChain=10&inputCurrency=&outputCurrency=&dlnMode=simple)
    
*   [Synapse Protocol](https://synapseprotocol.com/)
    
*   More: [Bridges: transfer funds between chains in the world of DeFi](https://talk.markets/t/bridges-transfer-funds-between-chains-in-the-world-of-defi/68)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/bnb-chain-bsc-cheatsheet/72#p-96-dex-5)

=====================================================================

     - Pumpfun for BSC

# How to chart DeFi tokens? - Crypto & DeFi - Talk.Markets

[How to chart DeFi tokens?](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-chart-defi-tokens/73)

================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Crypto & DeFi](https://talk.markets/c/guides/crypto/16)

[cp](https://talk.markets/tag/cp)

[Talk.Markets](https://talk.markets/u/Talk.Markets)  10 June 2021 20:26 1

There are numerous dApps available for charting, with each offering its own features. Most of these dApps now support multiple chains.

[](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-chart-defi-tokens/73#p-100-recommended-1)
Recommended
======================================================================================

*   [Photon](https://photon-sol.tinyastro.io/@RickBurpBot)
     ![:sol:](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/4/4871e9fc071dc845d033bcbc5807ddf0be63bbae.png?v=15 ":sol:")
*   [DexScreener](https://dexscreener.com/)
    
*   [Defined](https://defined.fi/)
    
*   [DexTools](https://dextools.io/app)
    
*   [GeckoTerminal](https://geckoterminal.com/)
    
*   [DexSpy](https://dexspy.io/)
     ![:eth:](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/1X/9025899848b7be0994967f6147642aa7022a5d36.png?v=15 ":eth:")

[](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-chart-defi-tokens/73#p-100-multichain-2)
Multichain
====================================================================================

*   [DexView](https://www.dexview.com/)
    
*   [DexGuru](https://dex.guru/)
    
*   [CoinBrain](https://coinbrain.com/)
    
*   [CoinScan](https://www.coinscan.com/)
    
*   [PooCoin](https://poocoin.app/)
     ![:bsc:](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/1X/14dca30620cfa6770a80af9a6c983f3841ba69f2.png?v=15 ":bsc:")

[Talk.Markets](https://talk.markets/u/Talk.Markets)  18 March 2021 13:51 1

Welcome, stranger! ![:wave:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/wave.png?v=15 ":wave:")

You came here because you show _some kind of_ interest in trading crypto/NFTs or other financial markets.

Talk.Markets strives to be a modern board for in-depth research, discussion, and information on cryptocurrencies like Bitcoin or [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
, DeFi, NFTs, as well as legacy markets like gold, oil, stocks, and forex.

> \[!rick\] This is also the home for [Rick Bot](https://talk.markets/c/rick/61)
>  documentation.

Our goals ![:railway_track:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/railway_track.png?v=15 ":railway_track:")

*   Share the stuff that matters, so we save ourselves some valuable time.
*   Maintain an accessible knowledge base for the community.

If you’re new to investing or trading, you have come to the right place. Sharing knowledge is key; start today. No days should pass where you don’t learn or discover anything new. You can also join our Discord - [see why](https://talk.markets/t/alpha-pack-discord-server/155)
.

Sign up for a free account for full access and participate to get the most out of this board - [How to register?](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-sign-up/176)

# How to invite friends? - forum tips - Talk.Markets

[How to invite friends?](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-invite-friends/77)

==========================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [forum tips](https://talk.markets/c/guides/forum-tips/51)

[Harvey](https://talk.markets/u/Harvey)  12 June 2021 23:15 1

To maintain high quality standards, we only allow limited invites per current user.

Every member can create **one** invite each day. Each invite can be used **two** times. This means you can invite two friends each day.

[](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-invite-friends/77#p-108-how-to-create-an-invite-link-1)
How to create an invite link?
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ![:fast_forward:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/fast_forward.png?v=15 ":fast_forward:") You can also follow [this link](https://talk.markets/my/invited/pending)

Click your avatar on the right top, then select the right tab with the user icon: ![:bust_in_silhouette:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/bust_in_silhouette.png?v=15 ":bust_in_silhouette:")

Then click Invites and click the Create button.

Send that link to your friends.

[How to sign up?](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-sign-up/176)

# KCC Mainnet [cheatsheet] - Chains - Talk.Markets

[KCC Mainnet \[cheatsheet\]](https://talk.markets/t/kcc-mainnet-cheatsheet/93)

===============================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Chains](https://talk.markets/c/guides/chains/39)

[cheatsheet](https://talk.markets/tag/cheatsheet)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   15 June 2021 21:39 1

KCC is a decentralized, high-performance, and low-cost public blockchain developed by the fans of [KuCoin](https://www.kucoin.com/ucenter/signup?rcode=E3m8gj)
 and KCS ([KuCoin](https://www.kucoin.com/ucenter/signup?rcode=E3m8gj)
 Token) to provide community users with a faster, more convenient, and low-cost blockchain experience.

[](https://talk.markets/t/kcc-mainnet-cheatsheet/93#p-128-metamask-rpc-details-1)
Metamask RPC Details
======================================================================================================

In Metamask go to Settings > Network and add the following information to get on [KuCoin](https://www.kucoin.com/ucenter/signup?rcode=E3m8gj)
 Community Chain (KCC) network.

*   **Network name**: KCC Mainnet
*   **RPC URL**: `https://rpc-mainnet.kcc.network`
*   **ChainID**: 321
*   **Symbol**: KCS
*   **Block Explorer**: `https://explorer.kcc.io/en/`

> ![:monkey:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/monkey.png?v=15 ":monkey:") [How to find KCC shitcoins](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-find-kcc-shitcoins/133)

[](https://talk.markets/t/kcc-mainnet-cheatsheet/93#p-128-bridge-2)
[Bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)

====================================================================================================================

*   [Official bridge](https://bridge.kcc.io/)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/kcc-mainnet-cheatsheet/93#p-128-charting-3)
Charting
==============================================================================

*   [Dexscreener](https://dexscreener.com/kcc)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/kcc-mainnet-cheatsheet/93#p-128-explorers-4)
Explorers
================================================================================

*   [KCC Explorer](https://explorer.kcc.io/en)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/kcc-mainnet-cheatsheet/93#p-128-charting-5)
Charting
==============================================================================

*   [MojitoSwap](https://app.mojitoswap.finance/swap)
    
*   [Koffeeswap](https://koffeeswap.exchange/#/pro)
     - Includes chart
*   [KuSwap](https://kuswap.finance/)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/kcc-mainnet-cheatsheet/93#p-128-info-6)

[Talk.Markets](https://talk.markets/u/Talk.Markets)   10 June 2021 15:09 1

[![image](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/9/9d9a157df01cb74233ed94fc1b37e021921937d1.png)\
\
image378×133 2.95 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/9/9d9a157df01cb74233ed94fc1b37e021921937d1.png "image")

> \[!notice\] As of **2025**, Polygon began transitioning to using the **POL** token instead of the old MATIC token. You can swap them for free [here](https://portal.polygon.technology/pol-upgrade)

In Metamask go to Settings > Network and add the following information to get on Polygon network.

[](https://talk.markets/t/polygon-network-cheatsheet/70#p-93-network-details-1)
Network Details
===============================================================================================

*   **Network Name:** Polygon Network
*   **RPC URL:** [polygon-mainnet.infura.io](http://polygon-mainnet.infura.io/)
    
*   **Chain ID:** `137`
*   **Currency Symbol:** `POL`
*   **Block Explorer URL:** [polygonscan.com](http://polygonscan.com/)
    

[](https://talk.markets/t/polygon-network-cheatsheet/70#p-93-bridge-2)

*   [cBridge](https://cbridge.celer.network/137/1/USDC)
