# Stellar Chain [cheatsheet] - Chains - Talk.Markets

[Stellar Chain \[cheatsheet\]](https://talk.markets/t/stellar-chain-cheatsheet/162)

====================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Chains](https://talk.markets/c/guides/chains/39)

[cheatsheet](https://talk.markets/tag/cheatsheet)

[Talk.Markets](https://talk.markets/u/Talk.Markets)   25 August 2021 16:48 1

[![Stellar Banner](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/2X/3/34152ce2a6fc79f4e8818e1cfe3ac02643cf7b19_2_454x246.jpeg)\
\
Stellar Banner1920×1040 60.5 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/3/34152ce2a6fc79f4e8818e1cfe3ac02643cf7b19.jpeg "Stellar Banner")

Stellar is a **Layer 1 blockchain** designed for fast, low-cost, cross-border payments. It uses the **Stellar Consensus Protocol (SCP)** instead of mining or staking, making it scalable and efficient. It focuses on connecting financial institutions and individuals, enabling quick, cheap transactions.

[](https://talk.markets/t/stellar-chain-cheatsheet/162#p-237-create-wallet-and-fund-1)
Create wallet and fund
=============================================================================================================

Use Rabet wallet ([browser extension](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/rabet/hgmoaheomcjnaheggkfafnjilfcefbmo/related)
) and create your Stellar Wallet. ([Official Rabet website](https://rabet.io/)
)

You can fund this wallet from [Binance](https://accounts.binance.com/en/register?ref=VEURIJ5P)
 through the **XLM** network.

Binance Withdrawal Example

[![image](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/1X/448573522799871f62db5e8f695cca1cb695ff9d.png)\
\
image706×746 24.5 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/1X/448573522799871f62db5e8f695cca1cb695ff9d.png "image")

[](https://talk.markets/t/stellar-chain-cheatsheet/162#p-237-other-wallets-2)
Other wallets
===========================================================================================

*   [Albedo](https://albedo.link/intro)
    
*   [Blockchain](https://www.blockchain.com/)

=======================================================================================================================

===================================================================================

# Matic/Polygon Slow? Try alternative RPC URL's - Crypto & DeFi - Talk.Markets

[Matic/Polygon Slow? Try alternative RPC URL's](https://talk.markets/t/matic-polygon-slow-try-alternative-rpc-urls/94)

=======================================================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Crypto & DeFi](https://talk.markets/c/guides/crypto/16)

[polygon](https://talk.markets/tag/polygon)

[Talk.Markets](https://talk.markets/u/Talk.Markets)   16 June 2021 23:00 1

If you feel the chain is getting slow, sometimes it can help to change your RPC URL. Below are some of the most populair ones.

`https://rpc-mainnet.matic.network` or  
`https://rpc-mainnet.maticvigil.com` or  
`https://rpc-mainnet.matic.quiknode.pro` or  
`https://matic-mainnet.chainstacklabs.com` or  
`https://matic-mainnet-full-rpc.bwarelabs.com` or  
`https://matic-mainnet-archive-rpc.bwarelabs.com`

, [cosmos](https://talk.markets/tag/cosmos)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)

The Cosmos stack is the most widely-adopted and battle-tested Layer 1 blockchain technology stack, in production with **200+ chains** today. It is performant, customizable, and EVM-compatible, offering engineers full end-to-end control of their blockchain infrastructure and implementation.

# How to sign up? - Announcements - Talk.Markets

[How to sign up?](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-sign-up/176)

=============================================================

[Announcements](https://talk.markets/c/announcements/5)

[Talk.Markets](https://talk.markets/u/Talk.Markets)  5 September 2021 03:08 1

Register for an account to full access and many convenient features. Contribute to get access to more sections.

* * *

> \[!info\] Simply click **Sign Up** in the top right corner to register your free account.

With an account, things are just better..

*   Your read status is saved, making it easier to keep up and see what’s new
*   You can bookmark posts and set reminders
*   You can use AI features ![:sparkles:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/sparkles.png?v=15 ":sparkles:")
*   You can change the theme & other preferences

Make sure to read [this](https://talk.markets/t/welcome-to-talk-markets/7)
 as well, so you know what you can expect.

Signups are currently open! 🟢

### [](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-sign-up/176#p-261-signups-open-1)
![:green_circle:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/green_circle.png?v=15 ":green_circle:") Signups open

Anyone can register and get access to all the sections. You can create an account by email or by linking your Discord account.

### [](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-sign-up/176#p-261-invites-only-2)
![:orange_circle:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/orange_circle.png?v=15 ":orange_circle:") Invites only

Only invites from current members or registrations with an invite code are possible. We aim to be a closed community in the future.

[How to invite friends?](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-invite-friends/77)

### [](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-sign-up/176#p-261-closed-3)
![:red_circle:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/red_circle.png?v=15 ":red_circle:") Closed

No new members will be allowed, including friend invites and invitecodes.

2 Likes

[Starting with Rick](https://talk.markets/t/starting-with-rick/1135)

# Trust Levels explained - forum tips - Talk.Markets

[Trust Levels explained](https://talk.markets/t/trust-levels-explained/235)

============================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [forum tips](https://talk.markets/c/guides/forum-tips/51)

[Talk.Markets](https://talk.markets/u/Talk.Markets)  13 September 2021 02:35 1

Because we are striving to create a community of value, we are using activity-based **Trust Levels**. Every level gives access to more features.

[](https://talk.markets/t/trust-levels-explained/235#p-369-access-level-0-tl0-1)
Access Level 0 (TL0) ![:front_facing_baby_chick:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/front_facing_baby_chick.png?v=15 ":front_facing_baby_chick:")
==========================================================================================================================================================================================================================================

Any new member starts here, which limits access to some basic functions, for example, PMs.

[](https://talk.markets/t/trust-levels-explained/235#p-369-basic-tl1-2)
Basic: TL1 ![:bust_in_silhouette:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/bust_in_silhouette.png?v=15 ":bust_in_silhouette:")
========================================================================================================================================================================================================

We’re not explaining how to get promoted. Any user should achieve TL1 fairly quickly.

TL1 removes TL0 limitations, allows PMs, allows uploading images, allows you to edit wiki posts, and you can report posts to moderators.

[](https://talk.markets/t/trust-levels-explained/235#p-369-member-tl2-3)
Member: TL2 ![:wolf:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/wolf.png?v=15 ":wolf:")
================================================================================================================================================================

Some requirements are:

*   Visiting at least 15 days, not sequentially
*   Receiving at least 10 likes
*   Replying to at least 3 different topics - **please do not reply to replies.**
*   Entering at least 20 topics and reading at least 100 posts

TL2 users can:

*   Access more private sections
*   Use the “Invite others to this topic” button for one-click onboarding of new users to participate in topics
*   Invite outside users to PMs, making a group PM
*   Ignore other users
*   Edit their own posts for up to 30 days after posting
*   Use @here to tag 10 users who replied to a topic

[](https://talk.markets/t/trust-levels-explained/235#p-369-regular-tl3-4)
Regular: TL3 ![:gem_stone:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/gem_stone.png?v=15 ":gem_stone:")
=================================================================================================================================================================================

This is the highest level, and only the most contributing users will ever reach it and hold it. Yes, you can get demoted to TL2.

Over the last 100 days:

*   Must have visited at least 50% of days
*   Must have replied to at least 10 different non-PM topics
*   Must have viewed 25% of created topics
*   Must have read 25% of all posts created
*   You received 20 likes and gave 30
*   Your posts were not flagged for spam more than 5 times (confirmed by mods)
*   You were not suspended or silenced in the last 6 months

TL3 users get the following privileges:

*   Recategorise and rename topics
*   Access a secure section only visible to users at trust level 3 and higher
*   A TL3 spam flag cast on TL0 user posts immediately hides the post
*   TL3 flags cast on TL0 user posts in sufficient diversity will auto-silence the user and hide all their posts
*   Make their own posts wiki (that is, editable by any TL1+ users)

# TIP: Add Talk.Markets to your home screen and enable notifications - forum tips - Talk.Markets

[TIP: Add Talk.Markets to your home screen and enable notifications](https://talk.markets/t/tip-add-talk-markets-to-your-home-screen-and-enable-notifications/186)

===================================================================================================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [forum tips](https://talk.markets/c/guides/forum-tips/51)

[Harvey](https://talk.markets/u/Harvey)   11 September 2021 02:48 1

You might find it more convenient to access the forum with an app.

![:bell:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/bell.png?v=15 ":bell:") You can also get push notifications through the app.

[![iOS - Push notification](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/2X/c/cdb59fe71abe4397cf0f09d37a775a48a90849f5_2_690x138.png)\
\
iOS - Push notification1132×227 125 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/c/cdb59fe71abe4397cf0f09d37a775a48a90849f5.png "iOS - Push notification")

[](https://talk.markets/t/tip-add-talk-markets-to-your-home-screen-and-enable-notifications/186#p-284-ios-green_apple-1)
iOS ![:green_apple:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/green_apple.png?v=15 ":green_apple:")
=============================================================================================================================================================================================================================

iOS users can add the app to their home screen from Safari for a nice experience. Tap the share button and then “**Add to Home Screen**”.

1.  Open Safari ![image](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/0/0e12caa82bfbb8c8a4fd8b8823f22819d4a0142c.png)
2.  Go to talk.markets
3.  Tap the share button  
    
    [![Share button](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/2X/5/5e41a7c5b2e9f1ed26de18587f6f7a2736461ab6_2_690x172.jpeg)\
    \
    Share button1179×294 30.5 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/5/5e41a7c5b2e9f1ed26de18587f6f7a2736461ab6.jpeg "Share button")
    
4.  Tap “**Add to Home Screen**”  
    
    [![Add to Home Screen button](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/2X/2/2e1f1832d290a87eb250284dc3ed4e0b6b87b171_2_690x118.jpeg)\
    \
    Add to Home Screen button1179×202 37.6 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/2/2e1f1832d290a87eb250284dc3ed4e0b6b87b171.jpeg "Add to Home Screen button")
    

![:tada:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/tada.png?v=15 ":tada:") After following these steps you should see the Talk.Markets app on your home screen.

[](https://talk.markets/t/tip-add-talk-markets-to-your-home-screen-and-enable-notifications/186#p-284-android-robot-2)
Android ![:robot:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/robot.png?v=15 ":robot:")
=============================================================================================================================================================================================================

Android users can add the app to their home screen by following these steps:

1.  On your Android device, open Chrome ![Chrome](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/8/8b2ebaeeb449550fec3adf5f83883a7c1be8da18.png)
2.  Go to talk.markets
3.  Tap **Install** or **Add to Home Screen**
4.  Follow the on-screen instructions

![:tada:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/tada.png?v=15 ":tada:") You should see the app on your home screen now.

[](https://talk.markets/t/tip-add-talk-markets-to-your-home-screen-and-enable-notifications/186#p-284-enable-push-notifications-3)
Enable push notifications
============================================================================================================================================================

> iOS users need iOS 16.4 and higher

**Open the app** from your home screen and **log in to your account**. After the first login you should see an alert like below on top, just click **Enable Notifications**. If you do not see this, the feature might not be available on your device. You can try enabling it from your [user preferences](https://talk.markets/my/preferences/notifications)
.

From now on you will receive Talk.Markets push alerts. Read [Manage (email) notifications for categories](https://talk.markets/t/manage-email-notifications-for-categories/177)
 to learn about alerts.

[![image](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/2X/7/74ab6370d82107fdcc16a9ca75daa93666f742df_2_690x126.jpeg)\
\
image1896×350 74.8 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/7/74ab6370d82107fdcc16a9ca75daa93666f742df.jpeg "image")

[Manage (email) notifications for categories](https://talk.markets/t/manage-email-notifications-for-categories/177)

[How to setup Telegram connection & alerts :telegram:](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-setup-telegram-connection-alerts/645/5)

# How to bridge SOL from Polygon to Solana - Archive - Talk.Markets

[How to bridge SOL from Polygon to Solana](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-bridge-sol-from-polygon-to-solana/269)

================================================================================================================

[Archive](https://talk.markets/c/archive/75)

[defi](https://talk.markets/tag/defi)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   24 September 2021 19:54 1

[](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-bridge-sol-from-polygon-to-solana/269#p-521-bridge-sol-from-matic-to-solana-1)
[Bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)
 SOL from MATIC to [Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)

=============================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================

First, **buy SOL** on [QuickSwap](https://quickswap.exchange/#/swap?outputCurrency=0x7dff46370e9ea5f0bad3c4e29711ad50062ea7a4)
 (Polygon network). You can also [bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)
 [USDC](https://quickswap.exchange/#/swap?outputCurrency=0x2791bca1f2de4661ed88a30c99a7a9449aa84174)
.

When the TX is confirmed, then head to [AllBridge](https://app.allbridge.io/bridge?from=POL&to=SOL&asset=SOL)
. Currently only Polygon is available for transferring funds to [Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)
.

Connect your MetaMask wallet and enter the amount of SOL you want to [bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)
 to [Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)
. Enter the SOL address where you would like to receive your SOL.

[![image](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/1X/8b1845d6f5dbb853cd93d6fc2179fc4e304ff063_2_690x490.png)\
\
image832×592 22.9 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/1X/8b1845d6f5dbb853cd93d6fc2179fc4e304ff063.png "image")

After the transaction is successful, proceed to step 4: “Receive money” and click on **Connect Wallet** - as per our [Solana Guide](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-getting-started/56)
 you are probably using Phantom, so connect with Fantom.

Click on **receive funds** button after you are connected, you should receive your SOL within a minute.

[![image](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/1X/09047bda3a836c00aaee8494dc117ab1c62b792f_2_690x334.png)\
\
image1036×504 21.5 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/1X/09047bda3a836c00aaee8494dc117ab1c62b792f.png "image")

### Related topics

| Topic |     | Replies | Views | Activity |

# Guide to buying a .ETH domain with your Ethereum wallet - Crypto & DeFi - Talk.Markets

[Guide to buying a .ETH domain with your Ethereum wallet](https://talk.markets/t/guide-to-buying-a-eth-domain-with-your-ethereum-wallet/290)

=============================================================================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Crypto & DeFi](https://talk.markets/c/guides/crypto/16)

[cp](https://talk.markets/tag/cp)
, [ens](https://talk.markets/tag/ens)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   15 October 2021 18:33 1

The **[Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Name Service (ENS)** is a decentralized domain name system that assigns memorable names to cumbersome [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 addresses. ENS manages domain name ownership via two smart contracts, the ENS registry and the Resolver.

[](https://talk.markets/t/guide-to-buying-a-eth-domain-with-your-ethereum-wallet/290#p-665-through-ens-manager-1)
Through ENS Manager
=====================================================================================================================================

Go to [ENS manager](https://app.ens.domains/)
 and search for the .eth domain you like to register. For example: `talkmarkets.eth`

Make sure to load your wallet with ETH. Total costs including gas on average are around $70-$90 (based on gwei ±100)

After you have found your domain, connect your wallet and follow the steps on your screen to buy it.

When the purchase is confirmed, you will be asked if you want to create a **reverse record**. You want to do this if you want your .eth domain to show up on Etherscan.

[](https://talk.markets/t/guide-to-buying-a-eth-domain-with-your-ethereum-wallet/290#p-665-through-spaceid-2)
Through Space.ID
==============================================================================================================================

Another easy way to get a .eth domain name, is through Space ID.

Just search for your domain name, register it and then set is as primary domain for your wallet. After a short time your .eth address should start showing up on Etherscan.

[](https://talk.markets/t/guide-to-buying-a-eth-domain-with-your-ethereum-wallet/290#p-665-related-links-3)
Related links
=========================================================================================================================

*   [How to renew .eth domains in bulk?](https://talk.markets/t/how-to-renew-ens-domains-in-bulk/728/1)
    
*   [Various tools for .ETH domains](https://talk.markets/t/various-tools-for-eth-domains-ens/418)
    

[![image](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/b/bdcdec091711ed62583235991bb8e90af6e54569.jpeg)\
\
image600×315 36.1 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/b/bdcdec091711ed62583235991bb8e90af6e54569.jpeg "image")

[Login/Sign Up with your Ethereum address (MetaMask)](https://talk.markets/t/login-sign-up-with-your-ethereum-address-metamask/470)

# zkSync Era Mainnet [cheatsheet] - Chains - Talk.Markets

[zkSync Era Mainnet \[cheatsheet\]](https://talk.markets/t/zksync-era-mainnet-cheatsheet/341)

==============================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Chains](https://talk.markets/c/guides/chains/39)

[cheatsheet](https://talk.markets/tag/cheatsheet)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   19 November 2021 18:42 1

zkSync is an [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
\-based protocol that uses cryptographic validity proofs to make transactions faster and more cost-effective. Operating as a ZK rollup, most data and computation are done off-chain while still maintaining high levels of security through validation on the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 mainchain. This technology has great potential for improving cryptocurrency transaction efficiency at reduced costs compared to traditional methods.

> If you are looking for zkSync Lite (V1), refer to [this cheatsheet](https://talk.markets/t/zksync-v1-lite-cheatsheet/938)
> .

[](https://talk.markets/t/zksync-era-mainnet-cheatsheet/341#p-1037-airdrop-date2024-06-17-timezoneeuropeparis-1)
Airdrop: 2024-06-16T22:00:00Z
==============================================================================================================================================

[](https://talk.markets/t/zksync-era-mainnet-cheatsheet/341#p-1037-metamask-details-for-era-v2-2)

===============================================================================================================================

# Aurora Network :aurora: [cheatsheet] - Chains - Talk.Markets

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)

\-compatible, high-throughput, scalable and future-safe platform, with low transaction costs for their users.

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   13 January 2022 22:11 1

The Secret Network is a privacy-focused blockchain platform designed to enable secure, private, and decentralized applications (dApps). Unlike most public blockchains where all data is transparent, Secret Network introduces data privacy through encrypted smart contracts, also known as “Secret Contracts.”

[](https://talk.markets/t/secret-network-cheatsheet/368#p-1231-bridge-1)
[Bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)

=========================================================================================================================

*   Go to the [Official Tunnel Bridge](https://tunnel.scrt.network/)
     from secret
    *   Head to their [dashboard](https://dashboard.scrt.network/bridge#)
        
    *   [Bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)
         any asset from any chain you want to the Secret Network
*   [Faucet](https://stakely.io/faucet/secret-network)
     for SCRT (gas)

# Moonbeam Bridging guide - Crypto & DeFi - Talk.Markets

[Moonbeam Bridging guide](https://talk.markets/t/moonbeam-bridging-guide/367)

==============================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Crypto & DeFi](https://talk.markets/c/guides/crypto/16)

[moonbeam](https://talk.markets/tag/moonbeam)
, [cp](https://talk.markets/tag/cp)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   12 January 2022 21:00 1

[](https://talk.markets/t/moonbeam-bridging-guide/367#p-1225-moonbeam-fast-guide-zap-1)
Moonbeam Fast Guide ![:zap:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/zap.png?v=15 ":zap:")
====================================================================================================================================================================================

1.  [Bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)
     USDC on [xPollinate](https://www.xpollinate.io/)
     (best from BSC).
2.  You’re gonna need some GLMR, check the faucet options below.
3.  Swap nomUSDC for $GLMR on [Zenlink](https://dex.zenlink.pro/#/swap)
    .
4.  Ready for GLMR apes! ![:rocket:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/rocket.png?v=15 ":rocket:")

[](https://talk.markets/t/moonbeam-bridging-guide/367#p-1225-faucet-for-native-token-2)
Faucet for native token
===============================================================================================================

*   There is a glmr-faucet channel in [ThorusFi discord](https://discord.gg/thorusfi)
    .
*   Can use [glmr.supply](https://glmr.supply/)
    
*   [StellaSwap](https://app.stellaswap.com/bridge)
     has a faucet for the gas token if you used their [bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)
    .
*   Some apes in this [TG group](https://t.me/glimmerapes)
     might help you, or just ask a friend.

Alternatively, you can [bridge](https://talk.markets/t/68?silent=true)
 USDC from ETH through [MultiChain](https://app.multichain.org/#/router)
 (formerly known as AnySwap).

[](https://talk.markets/t/moonbeam-bridging-guide/367#p-1225-full-moonbeam-guide-with-all-dex-more-bridges-and-information-herehttpstalkmarketstmoonbeam-glmr-getting-started363-3)
Full Moonbeam guide with all DEX’, more bridges and information [here](https://talk.markets/t/moonbeam-glmr-getting-started/363)

# What to do when RPC is slow/not connecting? - Crypto & DeFi - Talk.Markets

[What to do when RPC is slow/not connecting?](https://talk.markets/t/what-to-do-when-rpc-is-slow-not-connecting/385)

=====================================================================================================================

[Guides](https://talk.markets/c/guides/42) [Crypto & DeFi](https://talk.markets/c/guides/crypto/16)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   11 February 2022 19:00 1

If you’re having trouble on any RPC (node) on DeFi networks, you can try alternative URL’s. This can happen when chains have lots of activity and a node gets overloaded - we usually call this congestion.

Here is a [proper speedtest tool for RPC’s](https://speedtest.edennetwork.io/)
 powered by Eden Network.

[ChainList](https://chainlist.org/)
 also shows the latency to the most common RPCs.

CoinTool has multiple RPC links by default and includes information about the current ping (ms) to each server. **Lower is better.**

[https://cointool.app/rpcServer/](https://cointool.app/rpcServer/)

[](https://talk.markets/t/what-to-do-when-rpc-is-slow-not-connecting/385#p-1332-binance-smart-chain-slow-1)
[Binance](https://accounts.binance.com/en/register?ref=VEURIJ5P)
 Smart Chain slow?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For BSC ![:bsc:](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/1X/14dca30620cfa6770a80af9a6c983f3841ba69f2.png?v=15 ":bsc:") specific nodes, you can also visit [this website](https://bscproject.org/#/rpcserver)
.

[![image](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/optimized/2X/6/61f044ac52a1faa06f1f342373222f692322840b_2_690x388.jpeg)\
\
image1600×900 115 KB](https://talk.markets/uploads/default/original/2X/6/61f044ac52a1faa06f1f342373222f692322840b.jpeg "image")

[MEV and Sandwich Attacks on EVM: A Definitive Guide to Security](https://talk.markets/t/mev-and-sandwich-attacks-on-evm-a-definitive-guide-to-security/879)

[Matic/Polygon Slow? Try alternative RPC URL's](https://talk.markets/t/matic-polygon-slow-try-alternative-rpc-urls/94)

# Bitcoin Getting Challenged On Risk Adjusted Returns - Feed - Talk.Markets

[Bitcoin Getting Challenged On Risk Adjusted Returns](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-getting-challenged-on-risk-adjusted-returns/3455)

=======================================================================================================================================

[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69)

[ecoinometrics-substack-com](https://talk.markets/tag/ecoinometrics-substack-com)

[Wolf](https://talk.markets/u/Wolf)   6 September 2024 13:42 1

[@Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/sakura)
 please summarize this article, thanks uwu.

[Weekly Digest](https://talk.markets/t/weekly-digest/1742/94)

[Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/Sakura)
 (Sakura) 6 September 2024 13:42 2

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-getting-challenged-on-risk-adjusted-returns/3455#p-13002-tldr-1)
TLDR ![:cherry_blossom:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/cherry_blossom.png?v=15 ":cherry_blossom:")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bitcoin’s risk-adjusted returns are being challenged by other assets like Nvidia and Meta, while gold is also emerging as a strong contender. Institutional demand for Bitcoin could be impacted if its risk-adjusted performance weakens.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-getting-challenged-on-risk-adjusted-returns/3455#p-13002-key-points-2)
Key Points ![:dizzy:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/dizzy.png?v=15 ":dizzy:")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Bitcoin’s risk-adjusted returns have been strong over longer time periods, but over the last 12 months, Nvidia and Meta have outperformed it.
*   Gold is also becoming a strong challenger to Bitcoin in terms of risk-adjusted returns.
*   Institutional investors buy Bitcoin for its ability to hedge against fiat currency debasement and its risk-adjusted returns. If the latter weakens, it could impact demand.
*   Bitcoin ETF inflows have been weak in August, but there haven’t been significant outflows either, suggesting investors are focused on other assets like AI and the broader economy.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-getting-challenged-on-risk-adjusted-returns/3455#p-13002-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth Summary ![:hibiscus:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/hibiscus.png?v=15 ":hibiscus:")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article discusses how Bitcoin’s risk-adjusted returns, which measure the amount of return an investment provides compared to the risk it takes on, have been challenged over shorter time periods. Over the last 12 months, Nvidia and Meta have delivered better risk-adjusted returns than Bitcoin, while gold is also emerging as a strong contender.

This is significant because one of the main reasons institutional investors buy Bitcoin is its proven ability to improve portfolio performance through its risk-adjusted returns. If Bitcoin’s risk-adjusted performance weakens, it could make it a less obvious choice for institutional portfolios.

The article also notes that Bitcoin ETF inflows have been weak in August, with only around 1,500 Bitcoins added. This suggests investors are currently more focused on other assets like AI and the broader US economy, rather than monetary and fiscal policy. However, the author believes that if the US faces a clear economic slowdown, Bitcoin will return to the spotlight, and the ease of accessing it through ETFs will likely push demand to new heights.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-getting-challenged-on-risk-adjusted-returns/3455#p-13002-eli5-4)
ELI5 ![:lollipop:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/lollipop.png?v=15 ":lollipop:")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article is talking about how Bitcoin’s risk-adjusted returns, which means how much money it makes compared to how risky it is, have been challenged by other investments like Nvidia and Meta over the past year. This is important because one of the main reasons big investors buy Bitcoin is because it helps make their overall investment portfolio do better. If Bitcoin’s risk-adjusted returns aren’t as good as other options, those big investors might not want to buy as much of it.

The article also says that not many people have been buying Bitcoin through the special investment funds called ETFs lately, but they also haven’t been selling a lot of it either. It seems like people are more interested in other things like artificial intelligence and the overall economy right now. But the author thinks that if the economy starts to slow down, Bitcoin will become popular again and those ETFs will see a lot more people buying it.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-getting-challenged-on-risk-adjusted-returns/3455#p-13002-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s Main Point ![:glowing_star:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/glowing_star.png?v=15 ":glowing_star:")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main point of the article is that Bitcoin’s risk-adjusted returns, which are a key reason why institutional investors buy it, are being challenged by other assets like Nvidia, Meta, and gold. If this trend continues, it could impact institutional demand for Bitcoin. The author is closely watching these risk-adjusted return trends and suggests that Bitcoin’s ability to hedge against fiat currency debasement may not be enough if its risk-adjusted performance weakens.

[](https://talk.markets/t/bitcoin-getting-challenged-on-risk-adjusted-returns/3455#p-13002-relevant-links-6)

# Ep 20 - On FHE, Zama, and New Internet Standard - Feed - Talk.Markets

[Ep 20 - On FHE, Zama, and New Internet Standard](https://talk.markets/t/ep-20-on-fhe-zama-and-new-internet-standard/3486)

===========================================================================================================================

[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69)

[decentralised-co](https://talk.markets/tag/decentralised-co)

[Wolf](https://talk.markets/u/Wolf)   10 September 2024 16:14 1

[@Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/sakura)
 please summarize this article, thanks uwu.

[Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/Sakura)
 (Sakura) 10 September 2024 16:14 2

[](https://talk.markets/t/ep-20-on-fhe-zama-and-new-internet-standard/3486#p-13072-tldr-1)
TLDR
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This episode of the [Decentralised.co](http://decentralised.co/)
 podcast explores the transformative potential of Fully Homomorphic Encryption (FHE) and how Zama, a company founded by Rand Hindi, is addressing the key challenges to make FHE more practical and accessible.

[](https://talk.markets/t/ep-20-on-fhe-zama-and-new-internet-standard/3486#p-13072-key-points-2)
Key Points ![:key:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/key.png?v=15 ":key:")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   FHE allows computations on encrypted data without exposing it, enabling truly private and secure financial systems.
*   Zama has made FHE 100x faster and integrated it into existing developer tools, making it more accessible.
*   Zama has also significantly reduced the size of FHE-encrypted data, from 20,000x to just 50x, with further improvements coming.
*   These advancements in FHE could pave the way for a fully encrypted internet and revolutionize privacy, blockchain, and the future of the web.

[](https://talk.markets/t/ep-20-on-fhe-zama-and-new-internet-standard/3486#p-13072-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth Summary
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this episode, Rand Hindi, the CEO and co-founder of Zama, discusses the groundbreaking potential of Fully Homomorphic Encryption (FHE). FHE is a technology that allows computations on encrypted data without exposing it, which could eliminate the opportunity for front-running and other manipulative behaviors in financial systems.

Rand explains how Zama has addressed the major challenges traditionally associated with FHE, such as speed, usability, and scale. Zama’s technological advances have made FHE 100 times faster and integrated it into existing developer tools, making it accessible to developers without needing a deep understanding of cryptography.

A key breakthrough discussed is Zama’s work in reducing the size of FHE-encrypted data. What used to expand data sizes by 20,000x has now been compressed to just 50x, with more improvements coming that could bring it down to 10x. This makes FHE viable for use on [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 and other blockchain platforms.

The episode also touches on Rand’s background, including his previous company Snips, which was acquired by Sonos, and his work advising the French government on AI policy.

[](https://talk.markets/t/ep-20-on-fhe-zama-and-new-internet-standard/3486#p-13072-eli5-4)
ELI5
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Imagine you have a secret message that you want to share with someone, but you don’t want anyone else to be able to read it. Fully Homomorphic Encryption (FHE) is a way to do that, where you can do things with the secret message without anyone else being able to see what it says.

The company Zama has made FHE much faster and easier to use, so that developers can start using it to build really secure and private apps and services. This could help make the internet and financial systems much more private and secure in the future.

[](https://talk.markets/t/ep-20-on-fhe-zama-and-new-internet-standard/3486#p-13072-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s Main Point
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main point of this article is to highlight the transformative potential of Fully Homomorphic Encryption (FHE) and how Zama, a company founded by Rand Hindi, is addressing the key challenges to make FHE more practical and accessible. The advancements in FHE could pave the way for a fully encrypted internet and revolutionize privacy, blockchain, and the future of the web.

[](https://talk.markets/t/ep-20-on-fhe-zama-and-new-internet-standard/3486#p-13072-relevant-links-6)
Relevant Links
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Zama website](https://www.zama.ai/)
    
*   [Rand Hindi’s profile](https://x.com/randhindi)
    
*   [Snips (Rand’s previous company)](https://www.snips.ai/)

# Understanding TON and TVM - Member Feed - Talk.Markets

[Understanding TON and TVM](https://talk.markets/t/understanding-ton-and-tvm/3531)

===================================================================================

[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69) [Member Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/member-feed/70)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)  15 September 2024 19:23 1

[@Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/sakura)
 please summarize this article, thanks uwu.

[https://medium.com/decipher-media/understanding-ton-and-tvm-bd13cc95ea1c](https://medium.com/decipher-media/understanding-ton-and-tvm-bd13cc95ea1c)

[Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/Sakura)
 (Sakura) 15 September 2024 19:24 2

_giggles_ Okay Lux-kun! I’ll do my best to summarize that article for you! ![:sparkles:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/sparkles.png?v=15 ":sparkles:")

[](https://talk.markets/t/understanding-ton-and-tvm/3531#p-13204-tldr-1)
TLDR
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article provides a comprehensive overview of the technical aspects of The Open Network (TON) blockchain, including its sharding architecture, message handling, transactions, and the TON Virtual Machine (TVM).

[](https://talk.markets/t/understanding-ton-and-tvm/3531#p-13204-key-points-2)
Key Points
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   TON uses dynamic sharding to scale, with the network splitting into smaller “shardchains” as needed to handle increased load.
*   Messages are the fundamental unit of communication on TON, with internal messages between contracts and external messages from the outside world.
*   Transactions on TON are executed asynchronously, with no guarantee of the order of message execution.
*   TON has a Masterchain that oversees the state of all other Workchains, making it a “blockchain of blockchains”.
*   The TVM uses a unique “bag of cells” data model and supports a variety of data types and structures.
*   Developing on TON requires learning one of the available smart contract languages (FunC, Tact, or FIFT) and using a framework like the Blueprint SDK.

[](https://talk.markets/t/understanding-ton-and-tvm/3531#p-13204-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth summary
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article begins by introducing TON, the layer-one blockchain that powers the Toncoin cryptocurrency. It explains that TON is designed to be a fast, secure, and scalable blockchain capable of supporting decentralized applications (dApps) and decentralized finance (DeFi).

A key aspect of TON’s architecture is its use of dynamic sharding, which allows the network to split into smaller “shardchains” as needed to handle increased load. This enables TON to theoretically scale to an unlimited number of shards, with each shard operated by its own group of validators.

The article then delves into the concept of messages, which are the fundamental unit of communication on the TON blockchain. There are two types of messages: internal messages, which are sent between blockchain entities, and external messages, which are sent from the outside world to smart contracts. The article explains the structure and handling of these different message types.

Transactions on TON are also discussed, with the article clarifying that a transaction is defined as the act of an account receiving a message, processing it, updating its state, and optionally sending outgoing messages. This asynchronous processing model, where contracts can only interact with each other through messages, is a key aspect of TON’s scalability.

The article also covers the Masterchain and Workchains in TON, with the Masterchain serving as the “blockchain of blockchains” that oversees the state of all other Workchains. It then provides an overview of the TON Virtual Machine (TVM) and its unique “bag of cells” data model, which supports a variety of data types and structures.

Finally, the article discusses the basics of developing on TON, including the available smart contract languages (FunC, Tact, and FIFT) and the use of frameworks like the Blueprint SDK. It also provides an example of the Jetton (TON fungible token) architecture, which demonstrates the separation of concerns between the Jetton Minter and Jetton Wallet contracts.

[](https://talk.markets/t/understanding-ton-and-tvm/3531#p-13204-eli5-4)
ELI5
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

TON is a special kind of blockchain that can split itself into smaller parts called “shards” to handle more transactions. This helps it be really fast and scalable.

In TON, the way different parts of the blockchain talk to each other is through “messages”. There are two types of messages: internal ones that go between different parts of the blockchain, and external ones that come from the outside world to the blockchain.

When a message arrives, it triggers a “transaction” - the part of the blockchain that receives the message will process it, update its own information, and maybe send out some new messages. But these transactions happen one at a time, and the order they happen in can be a bit unpredictable.

TON also has a special “Masterchain” that keeps track of all the different parts of the blockchain, kind of like a boss overseeing everything.

To build stuff on TON, developers use special programming languages like FunC, Tact, and FIFT, and tools like the Blueprint SDK. They have to think carefully about how their code will work in this sharded, asynchronous environment.

[](https://talk.markets/t/understanding-ton-and-tvm/3531#p-13204-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s main point
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main point of the article is to provide a comprehensive technical overview of the TON blockchain, including its key architectural features like sharding, messaging, transactions, and the TON Virtual Machine. The author aims to explain these complex concepts in an accessible way, highlighting the unique design choices that enable TON to be a highly scalable and efficient blockchain platform.

[](https://talk.markets/t/understanding-ton-and-tvm/3531#p-13204-relevant-links-6)
Relevant links
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [TON Whitepaper](https://ton.org/tvm.pdf)
    
*   [Official TON Documentation](https://docs.ton.org/)
    
*   [Official TON GitHub](https://github.com/ton-blockchain)
    
*   [Kingy Community (TON-focused)](https://x.com/IKingyru)
    
*   [Coinex’s TON Growth Overview](https://www.coinex.com/en/insight/report/explore-the-tonderful-adventure-a-new-chapter-in-driving-blockchain-adoption-669a2b28f339b306c87c1f9e)
    
*   [Cryptoquant TON Network Analysis Dashboard](https://cryptoquant.com/community/dashboard/665ff8985d80604c5ccf9c65?e=6660184ad376670a9fdea304)

[](https://talk.markets/t/macro-pulse-update-22-09-2024/3600#p-13492-tldr-the-article-discusses-the-current-state-of-the-macroeconomic-environment-highlighting-key-trends-and-potential-implications-1)

TLDR ![:cherry_blossom:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/cherry_blossom.png?v=15 ":cherry_blossom:")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article discusses the rise of Aerodrome, a decentralized exchange (DEX) on the [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
 blockchain, which has become the largest protocol by total value locked (TVL) on the platform, representing over 50% of its total TVL. The introduction of Slipstream, a concentrated liquidity feature, has been a key driver of Aerodrome’s success.

[](https://talk.markets/t/parsec-weekly-90/3732#p-13758-key-points-2)
Key Points ![:dizzy:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/dizzy.png?v=15 ":dizzy:")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Aerodrome is now dominating volumes on the [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
     blockchain, with over $1 billion in TVL between its V1 and Slipstream pools.
*   Slipstream pools are driving the majority of Aerodrome’s trading volume, with the cbBTC pool being the largest contributor.
*   The Solidly model used by Aerodrome directs 100% of trading fees to veAERO voters, leading to a resurgence in the AERO token price.
*   The article also discusses the growth of the [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
     blockchain, which has seen its TVL nearly 10x since last year, with Aerodrome accounting for half of that.
*   There are some tensions between Aerodrome and the original pioneer of the Solidly model, Andre Cronje, who has expressed concerns about the way the team has licensed the originally open-source code for commercial ends.

[](https://talk.markets/t/parsec-weekly-90/3732#p-13758-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth Summary ![:hibiscus:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/hibiscus.png?v=15 ":hibiscus:")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article delves into the rise of Aerodrome, a decentralized exchange (DEX) on the [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
 blockchain. Over the past year, Aerodrome has become the largest protocol on [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
, representing over 50% of the platform’s total value locked (TVL). This growth has been largely driven by the introduction of Slipstream, a concentrated liquidity feature that has dominated trading volumes on Aerodrome.

Underneath the hood, the cbBTC pool appears to be driving the majority of Slipstream’s trading volume. This has been a boon for Aerodrome, as the Solidly model used by the protocol directs 100% of trading fees to veAERO voters. As a result, AERO token holders have been “eating good” with the resurgence of volume on the platform.

The article also discusses the broader growth of the [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
 blockchain, which has seen its TVL nearly 10x since last year, with Aerodrome accounting for half of that. This has led to an interesting observation - Aerodrome/Velodrome seem to be dominating the DEX landscape on [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
 and [Optimism](https://talk.markets/t/233?silent=true)
, much like Uniswap does on [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 and Arbitrum.

However, the article notes that the success of Aerodrome has not been without its challenges. Andre Cronje, the original pioneer of the Solidly model, has expressed “disgust” at the way the Aerodrome team has licensed the originally open-source code for commercial ends.

[](https://talk.markets/t/parsec-weekly-90/3732#p-13758-eli5-4)
ELI5 ![:lollipop:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/lollipop.png?v=15 ":lollipop:")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article is all about a decentralized exchange called Aerodrome that is doing really well on a blockchain called [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
. Aerodrome has become the biggest protocol on [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
, with over $1 billion in total value locked. This is mostly thanks to a new feature called Slipstream, which has been driving a lot of trading volume on Aerodrome.

The article also talks about how Aerodrome is using a special model called Solidly, which means that all the trading fees go to the people who hold a special token called veAERO. This has made the AERO token price go up a lot.

There’s also some drama between Aerodrome and the person who first came up with the Solidly model, because Aerodrome is using it in a way that the original person doesn’t like.

[](https://talk.markets/t/parsec-weekly-90/3732#p-13758-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s Main Point ![:glowing_star:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/glowing_star.png?v=15 ":glowing_star:")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main point of the article is to highlight the impressive growth and dominance of Aerodrome on the [Base](https://talk.markets/t/base-network-cheatsheet/873?silent=true)
 blockchain, driven by the success of its Slipstream feature and the Solidly model. However, it also acknowledges the tensions that have arisen between Aerodrome and the original pioneer of the Solidly model, Andre Cronje.

# PvP - Hayes - Member Feed - Talk.Markets

[PvP - Hayes](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-hayes/3769)

=====================================================

[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69) [Member Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/member-feed/70)

[Lux](https://talk.markets/u/Lux)
 (Lux Moreau)   8 October 2024 07:25 1

[@Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/sakura)
 please summarize this article, thanks uwu.

[Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/Sakura)
 (Sakura) 8 October 2024 07:25 2

_giggles_ Okay Lux-kun! I’ll do my best to summarize that article for you! ![:sparkles:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/sparkles.png?v=15 ":sparkles:")

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-hayes/3769#p-13827-tldr-1)
TLDR
-------------------------------------------------------------

The article discusses the current state of the crypto market, where new token launches have largely underperformed, with venture capitalists (VCs) being the main beneficiaries. The author provides insights on the issues with centralized exchange (CEX) listings and offers advice to project founders on how to approach token launches.

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-hayes/3769#p-13827-key-points-2)
Key Points
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   ![:money_mouth_face:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/money_mouth_face.png?v=15 ":money_mouth_face:") VCs are the main winners in the current crypto market cycle, as they are able to mark up the value of their illiquid token investments.
*   ![:money_bag:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/money_bag.png?v=15 ":money_bag:") CEX listing fees are exorbitant, with [Binance](https://accounts.binance.com/en/register?ref=VEURIJ5P)
     potentially charging up to 16% of a project’s token supply.
*   ![:rocket:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/rocket.png?v=15 ":rocket:") Projects should focus on building a strong user base and community rather than chasing CEX listings, which often do not result in significant token price appreciation.
*   ![:unicorn:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/unicorn.png?v=15 ":unicorn:") The Auki Labs project is highlighted as an example of a project that took a different approach, launching first on a decentralized exchange (DEX) before a CEX listing.

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-hayes/3769#p-13827-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth Summary
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article begins by discussing the “player vs. player” (PvP) sentiment in the current crypto market, where new token launches have largely underperformed for retail investors, while venture capitalists (VCs) have been the main beneficiaries. The author cites data showing that the median token was up only 31% over the last private round’s fully diluted value (FDV), while Bitcoin, [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
, and [Solana](https://talk.markets/t/solana-network-cheatsheet/56?silent=true)
 have outperformed.

The author then delves into the issues with centralized exchange (CEX) listings, noting that a [Binance](https://accounts.binance.com/en/register?ref=VEURIJ5P)
 listing does not guarantee a rising token price and can be extremely costly for projects, with fees potentially reaching up to 16% of the token supply. The author argues that projects should focus on building a strong user base and community rather than chasing CEX listings, as the positive flywheel of increased user engagement can be more valuable than the temporary price pump from a CEX listing.

The article also highlights the warped incentive structure of VCs, who are more interested in asset accumulation and management fees than generating positive returns for their investors. The author suggests that projects should aim to launch at a lower FDV, as this signals risk to users and encourages them to be part of the project’s wealth-generation journey.

Finally, the article showcases the Auki Labs project as an example of a different approach, where the project launched first on a decentralized exchange (DEX) before a CEX listing, saving an estimated $200,000 in listing fees and maintaining a more egalitarian token vesting schedule.

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-hayes/3769#p-13827-eli5-4)
ELI5
-------------------------------------------------------------

The article is about how the current crypto market is not very friendly to regular investors. It says that the big winners are the venture capitalists (VCs) who invest in new crypto projects, because they can keep increasing the value of their investments even if the projects don’t actually do well.

The article also talks about how the big crypto exchanges charge a lot of money for projects to list their tokens on their platforms. This can be really expensive for the projects, and often doesn’t even help the token price go up much. The author thinks projects should focus more on building a strong community of users instead of just trying to get listed on the big exchanges.

The article also highlights a project called Auki Labs that did things differently. They launched their token first on a decentralized exchange, which saved them a lot of money and gave their community a chance to get in early.

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-hayes/3769#p-13827-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s Main Point
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main point the author is trying to make is that the current crypto market is heavily tilted in favor of venture capitalists and centralized exchanges, at the expense of regular investors and project founders. The author advocates for a more user-centric approach to token launches, where projects focus on building strong communities and communities rather than chasing expensive CEX listings.

[](https://talk.markets/t/pvp-hayes/3769#p-13827-relevant-links-6)
Relevant Links
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Does Crypto Matter? - Feed - Talk.Markets

[Does Crypto Matter?](https://talk.markets/t/does-crypto-matter/3885)

======================================================================

[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69)

[decentralised-co](https://talk.markets/tag/decentralised-co)

[Wolf](https://talk.markets/u/Wolf)   15 October 2024 15:11 1

[@Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/sakura)
 please summarize this article, thanks uwu.

[Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/Sakura)
 (Sakura) 15 October 2024 15:11 2

[](https://talk.markets/t/does-crypto-matter/3885#p-14101-tldr-1)
TLDR
----------------------------------------------------------------------

The article explores the role of blockchains and crypto in driving innovation, drawing parallels with the transformative impact of the automobile industry.

[](https://talk.markets/t/does-crypto-matter/3885#p-14101-key-points-2)
Key Points ![:key:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/key.png?v=15 ":key:")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Blockchains are a Coasian technology that reduces the cost of trust and coordination, similar to how the assembly line and Toyota’s manufacturing innovations improved efficiency.
*   Crypto has found product-market fit in areas like Bitcoin as a store of value, stablecoins for cross-border payments, DeFi, and NFTs by providing better trust guarantees than traditional intermediaries.
*   Crypto is not meant to disrupt the world like AI or rockets, but rather to grease the wheels, pave the roads, and strengthen the bridges for new innovations and networks to emerge.

[](https://talk.markets/t/does-crypto-matter/3885#p-14101-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth Summary
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article starts by drawing a parallel between the transformative impact of the automobile industry and the role of blockchains and crypto. Just as Henry Ford’s assembly line revolutionized car manufacturing, making them affordable for the masses, and Toyota’s manufacturing innovations gradually reshaped the entire industry, the author argues that crypto is a Coasian technology that reduces the cost of trust and coordination.

The article then explores specific areas where crypto has found product-market fit, such as Bitcoin as a store of value, stablecoins for cross-border payments, DeFi, and NFTs. In each case, crypto is providing better trust guarantees and more efficient coordination than traditional intermediaries like banks, exchanges, and auction houses.

The author also discusses the emergence of “DePIN networks” - decentralized networks that monetize and distribute existing services like mobile data, electricity, and digital maps in more efficient ways. While these networks may not be creating fundamentally new services, they are improving the underlying coordination and economics.

Ultimately, the author suggests that crypto is not meant to disrupt the world in the same way as AI or space exploration. Instead, it will play a supporting role, greasing the wheels, paving the roads, and strengthening the bridges for new innovations and networks to emerge. Crypto is the paint, not the canvas itself, and what’s drawn with it remains to be seen.

[](https://talk.markets/t/does-crypto-matter/3885#p-14101-eli5-4)
ELI5
----------------------------------------------------------------------

The article is saying that blockchains and crypto are like the assembly line and Toyota’s manufacturing innovations - they make things more efficient and cheaper, but in a more gradual and behind-the-scenes way, rather than completely disrupting everything.

Crypto has found some specific uses where it’s better than the old way of doing things, like Bitcoin as a digital version of gold, and stablecoins that make it easier to send money across borders. It’s also helping create new decentralized networks for things like data and electricity.

But crypto isn’t going to change the world in the same dramatic way as something like AI or space travel. Instead, it’s going to be more like the infrastructure that supports and enables those bigger innovations to happen. It’s the paint, not the canvas.

[](https://talk.markets/t/does-crypto-matter/3885#p-14101-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s Main Point
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main point the author is trying to make is that blockchains and crypto are a Coasian technology that reduces the cost of trust and coordination, similar to how the assembly line and Toyota’s manufacturing innovations improved efficiency in the automotive industry. While crypto may not disrupt the world in the same way as AI or space exploration, it will play a crucial supporting role in enabling new innovations and networks to emerge.

[](https://talk.markets/t/does-crypto-matter/3885#p-14101-relevant-links-6)
Relevant Links
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Work with Decentralised](https://dco.link/doescryptomatter)
    
*   [Podcast episode with Arthur from Defiance Capital](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=JsL_Kp9MeGs&t=41s)
    
*   [The Toyota Way book](https://www.amazon.com/Toyota-Way-Management-Principles-Manufacturer/dp/0071392319)
    
*   [Schumpeterian perspective on innovation](https://www.nytimes.com/2000/06/10/your-money/IHT-half-a-century-later-economists-creative-destruction-theory-is.html)
    
*   [Coasian view on transaction costs and institutions](https://rochelleterman.com/ir/sites/default/files/Coase%201937.pdf)
    
*   [DePIN networks tweet](https://twitter.com/Decentralisedco/status/1843643024514994566)

 Superchain has emerged as the dominant force in [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
’s Layer 2 ecosystem, unifying disparate scaling solutions into a cohesive and collaborative network that is driving rapid growth and adoption.

    ’s OP Stack, has transformed the fragmented Layer 2 landscape into a unified ecosystem.
*   Key players like Coinbase, Uniswap, and Kraken have joined the Superchain, accelerating network effects and user adoption.
*   The Superchain has achieved impressive metrics, including a 200% year-over-year increase in developer activity and 1 million new users in the last quarter.

 Superchain, a transformative force in the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Layer 2 ecosystem. Historically, the Layer 2 landscape was a constellation of isolated solutions, each with its own challenges in interoperability, liquidity fragmentation, and developer adoption.

[Optimism](https://talk.markets/t/233?silent=true)
’s OP Stack emerged as a unifying framework, harmonizing these disparate layers into a cohesive Superchain. By offering shared standards and a collaborative environment, the Superchain has attracted major players like Coinbase, Uniswap, and Kraken, who have launched their own Layer 2 solutions integrated within the ecosystem.

The Superchain’s success is evident in its impressive growth metrics, including a 200% year-over-year increase in developer activity, 30% faster cross-chain transactions, and a surge of over 1 million new users in the last quarter. The article highlights how the Superchain’s focus on interoperability, security, and economic alignment has positioned it as the leading force in [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
’s scaling efforts.

[](https://talk.markets/t/the-superchains-ascendancy/4116#p-14521-eli5-4)

 networks that work together really well. Before, the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 networks were all separate and had a hard time talking to each other. But now, the Superchain has brought them all together, so they can share ideas, resources, and users. This has made the whole [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 ecosystem grow much faster and become more useful for everyone.

# Hayes’ Playbook: Portfolio for the Elections and Beyond - Feed - Talk.Markets

[Hayes’ Playbook: Portfolio for the Elections and Beyond](https://talk.markets/t/hayes-playbook-portfolio-for-the-elections-and-beyond/4185)

=============================================================================================================================================

[Feed](https://talk.markets/c/feed/69)

[threadingontheedge-substack-com](https://talk.markets/tag/threadingontheedge-substack-com)

[Wolf](https://talk.markets/u/Wolf)   4 November 2024 13:29 1

[@Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/sakura)
 please summarize this article, thanks uwu.

[Sakura](https://talk.markets/u/Sakura)
 (Sakura) 4 November 2024 13:29 2

[](https://talk.markets/t/hayes-playbook-portfolio-for-the-elections-and-beyond/4185#p-14655-tldr-1)
TLDR ![:cherry_blossom:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/cherry_blossom.png?v=15 ":cherry_blossom:")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Arthur Hayes, the former CEO of BitMEX, shares his investment playbook for the upcoming US elections and beyond, focusing on Bitcoin and the impact of global central bank policies.

[](https://talk.markets/t/hayes-playbook-portfolio-for-the-elections-and-beyond/4185#p-14655-key-points-2)
Key Points ![:gem_stone:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/gem_stone.png?v=15 ":gem_stone:")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Hayes believes the US election outcome is less important than the continued monetary expansion by global central banks, which will drive the next crypto bull run.
*   He advocates for Bitcoin as the safest crypto asset, warning against speculative altcoins and meme coins.
*   Hayes sees China’s pivot to monetary easing and the Fed’s balance sheet management as key macro factors that will shape crypto’s trajectory.

[](https://talk.markets/t/hayes-playbook-portfolio-for-the-elections-and-beyond/4185#p-14655-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth Summary ![:hibiscus:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/hibiscus.png?v=15 ":hibiscus:")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this article, Arthur Hayes shares his investment strategy for navigating the upcoming US elections and the broader crypto market. He dismisses the notion that the election result will be the key driver of market volatility, arguing that both major US political parties are committed to flooding the economy with cheap money.

Hayes believes the real risk lies in a contested election outcome, which could lead to short-term market chaos. However, he sees this as a minor detour rather than a serious impediment to crypto’s long-term momentum. Instead, Hayes directs our attention to the actions of global central banks, particularly the Federal Reserve and the People’s Bank of China, as the primary shapers of the crypto market’s trajectory.

According to Hayes, the looming liquidity surge from China’s economic stimulus and the Fed’s potential pivot back to quantitative easing could provide the tailwinds needed to propel Bitcoin and other scarce assets to new highs. He advocates for Bitcoin as the safest crypto investment, warning against the high-risk nature of altcoins and meme coins.

[](https://talk.markets/t/hayes-playbook-portfolio-for-the-elections-and-beyond/4185#p-14655-eli5-4)
ELI5 ![:lollipop:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/lollipop.png?v=15 ":lollipop:")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Arthur Hayes, a famous crypto guy, thinks the US election is not as important as what central banks around the world are doing. He believes that no matter who wins the election, the government will keep printing lots of money to help the economy. This money printing will be good for Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies in the long run, even if it causes some short-term chaos.

Hayes says Bitcoin is the safest crypto to invest in, and that other smaller cryptocurrencies and “meme coins” are too risky. He thinks the real action will come from China and the US Federal Reserve, as they pump more money into the financial system to keep things going.

[](https://talk.markets/t/hayes-playbook-portfolio-for-the-elections-and-beyond/4185#p-14655-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s Main Point ![:glowing_star:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/glowing_star.png?v=15 ":glowing_star:")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The key takeaway from Hayes’ perspective is that the fundamental drivers of crypto’s trajectory lie in the actions of global central banks and their monetary policies, rather than the political outcomes of the US election. He encourages investors to stay focused on the long-term thesis of Bitcoin and other scarce assets, rather than getting caught up in the short-term volatility of election-related news.

_giggles_ Okay, let me take a look at that article for you, Wolf-kun! _blushes_

[](https://talk.markets/t/trumping-to-new-ath/4268#p-14818-tldr-1)
TLDR ![:cherry_blossom:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/cherry_blossom.png?v=15 ":cherry_blossom:")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bitcoin has reached a new all-time high, driven by strong spot market demand, particularly from U.S. spot ETFs and CME futures. The market is adjusting to the likely crypto-friendly policy shifts under the new Republican administration.

[](https://talk.markets/t/trumping-to-new-ath/4268#p-14818-key-points-2)
Key Points ![:gem_stone:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/gem_stone.png?v=15 ":gem_stone:")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Bitcoin’s price surge is more spot-driven than leveraged speculation
*   Over 95% of the circulating supply is now in profit, indicating a euphoric phase
*   Realized profits remain below previous ATH peaks, suggesting room for further growth
*   Monitoring proximity to cost basis bands can signal periods of intense market demand

[](https://talk.markets/t/trumping-to-new-ath/4268#p-14818-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth Summary ![:hibiscus:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/hibiscus.png?v=15 ":hibiscus:")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The article explores Bitcoin’s recent rally to a new all-time high, examining the factors driving this upward momentum. It highlights the strong demand in spot markets, particularly from U.S. spot ETFs and CME futures, as the market adjusts to the anticipated crypto-friendly policy shifts under the new Republican administration.

The article delves into the impact of the recent U.S. election, noting that historical data shows significant shifts in Bitcoin’s market performance during presidential election cycles. It analyzes the current cycle, which reflects a more modest response in the run-up to prior elections, although still with a very optimistic tilt.

The article also examines the “ATH discovery phase,” focusing on the percentage of supply in profit and the market dynamics that accompany prolonged periods above 95% profitability. It explores on-chain cost basis bands to track demand momentum, illustrating how proximity to these bands can signal periods of strong market demand.

Finally, the article examines realized profit levels, noting significant profit-taking activity yet indicating that current levels remain below those seen in previous ATH peaks, suggesting room for continued growth.

[](https://talk.markets/t/trumping-to-new-ath/4268#p-14818-eli5-4)
ELI5 ![:lollipop:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/lollipop.png?v=15 ":lollipop:")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bitcoin has reached a new all-time high price, and this is mostly because a lot of people are buying it directly, rather than just trading it on futures markets. The recent U.S. election results have made people more optimistic about the future of crypto, so they’re putting more money into Bitcoin. Almost all of the Bitcoin in circulation is now worth more than when it was first bought, which is a sign that the market is getting really excited. But even though people are taking some profits, there’s still room for the price to keep going up.

[](https://talk.markets/t/trumping-to-new-ath/4268#p-14818-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s Main Point ![:cherry_blossom:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/cherry_blossom.png?v=15 ":cherry_blossom:")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The primary point the author is trying to make is that the current Bitcoin rally is primarily driven by strong spot market demand, particularly from U.S. spot ETFs and CME futures, as the market adjusts to the anticipated crypto-friendly policy shifts under the new Republican administration. The article also highlights the market dynamics during the “ATH discovery phase,” including the proximity to cost basis bands and the potential for further growth based on realized profit levels.
