TLDR
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Foundation is launching its first formal summer internship program in 2025, offering opportunities for both research and development roles.

[](https://talk.markets/t/announcing-the-2025-ef-internship-program/4330#p-14896-key-points-2)
Key Points ![:key:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/key.png?v=15 ":key:")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The internship program aims to nurture the next generation of [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
     developers and researchers.
*   Interns will work alongside EF teams and contribute directly to core projects in areas like protocol security, account abstraction, scaling research, and client development.
*   The program is open to applicants who are familiar with the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
     protocol and available for full-time work, with a focus on advanced university students.
*   Interns can choose to work remotely or in one of the EF offices in Boulder (USA) or Berlin (Germany), and will be invited for an in-person cohort meetup.

[](https://talk.markets/t/announcing-the-2025-ef-internship-program/4330#p-14896-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth Summary
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Foundation is launching its first formal summer internship program in 2025, offering opportunities for both research and development roles. The program is aimed at nurturing the next generation of [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 developers and researchers, with interns working alongside EF teams and contributing directly to core projects.

Applicants should be familiar with the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 protocol and available for full-time work, with a focus on advanced university students. Interns will be assigned short-term projects and mentors, and can choose to work remotely or in one of the EF offices in Boulder (USA) or Berlin (Germany). In addition, interns will be invited for an in-person cohort meetup in the summer.

The internship program is distinct from the existing [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Protocol Fellowship, which is a six-month program that assumes advanced knowledge and a desire for full-time work in [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
. The internship is geared towards those with a general skillset and a desire to learn how to apply that skillset to the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 domain.

[](https://talk.markets/t/announcing-the-2025-ef-internship-program/4330#p-14896-eli5-4)
ELI5
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Foundation is starting a new summer program where people can come and work with the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 team for a few months. They’ll get to help with important [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 projects and learn a lot about how [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 works. It’s a great opportunity for people who are interested in [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 and want to get some hands-on experience.

[](https://talk.markets/t/announcing-the-2025-ef-internship-program/4330#p-14896-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s Main Point
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main point of the article is to announce the launch of the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Foundation’s first formal summer internship program in 2025, which will offer opportunities for both research and development roles. The program aims to nurture the next generation of [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 developers and researchers by allowing them to work alongside EF teams and contribute directly to core [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)

 Foundation is now accepting applications for the Next Billion Fellowship Program, which aims to find and support stories that showcase how [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 is helping communities address real-world challenges.

    ’s role in solving problems and creating meaningful change.

     network, and opportunities for exposure to the selected Fellows.

In-depth Summary

The [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Foundation is excited to announce that applications are now open for the Next Billion Fellowship Program. This program is a search for stories - real, human stories that showcase how [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 is being used to address the challenges faced by communities around the world.

The selected Fellows will receive project funding, mentorship, access to the [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 network, and opportunities for exposure. Past Fellows have worked on a wide range of projects, from implementing digital badges and wallets for millions of scouts worldwide to creating more efficient and affordable crop insurance for smallholder farmers in Kenya, and even exploring the role of decentralized systems during humanitarian crises in Syria.

The application process is open until January 12, 2025, with rolling applications considered for the subsequent Cohort 6. The current Cohort 5 will run from April to October 2025. The [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 Foundation is hosting two “Office Hours” sessions on December 11, 2024, and January 8, 2025, for those interested in learning more about the program.

 Foundation is looking for people with cool ideas on how to use [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 to help their communities. If you have a good idea, you can apply to their program, and if you get chosen, they will give you money and help you make your idea a reality. They want to find stories of how [Ethereum](https://talk.markets/t/ethereum-erc-20-cheatsheet/270?silent=true)
 is being used to solve real problems and make a difference in people’s lives.

[](https://talk.markets/t/next-billion-fellowship-program-applications-now-open/4544#p-15216-writers-main-point-5)

 is being used to address real-world challenges and create meaningful change in communities around the world.

_giggles_ Okay Lux-kun! I’ll do my best to summarize that article for you! ![:sparkles:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/sparkles.png?v=15 ":sparkles:")

[](https://talk.markets/t/safenet-launches-revolutionizing-defi-to-move-100-trillion-global-economy/4694#p-15552-tldr-1)
TLDR
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Safenet is a revolutionary transaction processor network that aims to revolutionize DeFi by streamlining blockchain transactions, taking inspiration from VisaNet. It unbundles transaction execution and settlement, bringing execution guarantees to onchain transactions.

[](https://talk.markets/t/safenet-launches-revolutionizing-defi-to-move-100-trillion-global-economy/4694#p-15552-key-points-2)
Key Points ![:key:](https://talk.markets/images/emoji/twitter/key.png?v=15 ":key:")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Safenet is not a blockchain or layer 2, but a transaction processor network that works on top of any existing or future chain
*   It has two core components: Processors and a Liquidity Network
*   Safenet is designed to enable an economy of different application-specific processors, unlocking new business models
*   It has a decentralized validator network to strengthen security

[](https://talk.markets/t/safenet-launches-revolutionizing-defi-to-move-100-trillion-global-economy/4694#p-15552-in-depth-summary-3)
In-depth Summary
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Safenet is a novel transaction processor network that aims to revolutionize the decentralized finance landscape. It takes inspiration from VisaNet, the payment processing network that connects different financial institutions to facilitate fast, secure payments globally.

Safenet brings a similar architecture to onchain transactions in a decentralized way. It unbundles the execution guarantee and settlement of a transaction, allowing for faster speeds (under 500ms even for cross-chain transactions), enhanced security through user-defined policies, and scalability across diverse ecosystems.

The core components of Safenet are Safenet Processors, which act as execution nodes, and the Safenet Liquidity Network, which provides the required liquidity to execute transaction intents. Safenet is designed to enable an economy of different application-specific processors, unlocking new business models around onchain transactions, such as off-exchange settlement, loans, and subscriptions.

To strengthen the security of Safenet, a decentralized validator network monitors the activity of processors and can trigger challenges if any transactions are triggered maliciously or not in compliance with user-set policies. The SAFE token underpins the economic model, aligning incentives across the ecosystem.

[](https://talk.markets/t/safenet-launches-revolutionizing-defi-to-move-100-trillion-global-economy/4694#p-15552-eli5-4)
ELI5
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Safenet is like a super-fast, super-secure way to do transactions on the blockchain. It’s not a blockchain itself, but a network that works on top of other blockchains to make transactions happen really quickly and safely. It’s kind of like how Visa works, but for the blockchain world. Safenet has special “processors” that can execute transactions instantly, and a network of “validators” that make sure everything is working properly. It’s all designed to help move the whole world’s economy onto the blockchain!

[](https://talk.markets/t/safenet-launches-revolutionizing-defi-to-move-100-trillion-global-economy/4694#p-15552-writers-main-point-5)
Writer’s Main Point
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main point of the article is to introduce Safenet, a novel transaction processor network that aims to revolutionize the decentralized finance landscape by streamlining blockchain transactions and bringing execution guarantees to onchain transactions, taking inspiration from VisaNet. Safenet is designed to enable an economy of different application-specific processors, unlocking new business models and use cases for onchain transactions.

[](https://talk.markets/t/safenet-launches-revolutionizing-defi-to-move-100-trillion-global-economy/4694#p-15552-relevant-links-6)
Relevant Links
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
